structure.\\n      - Manifest digest MUST be computed over exact manifest JSON bytes written to CAS.\\n  - Manifest serialization:\\n      - MUST be stable JSON with deterministic key ordering and commits even when canonical state is unchanged.\\n      - The system MUST therefore compute and record \`semantic\_manifest\_digest\` as the stable comparison key:\\n          - state” MUST use \`semantic\_manifest\_digest\`\\n            \(and \`ept\_digest\`\), not \`manifest\_digest\`.\\n      - The manifest MUST record both:\\n          - \`manifest\_digest\` \(CAS digest expected\_head = H\\n    Then the commit fails with HeadMismatch\\n    And no new ledger row is appended\\n\\n  Scenario: Commit is safe when called concurrently with the same expected\_head\\n And snapshot commit fails with DeterminismViolation \(unless waived by policy\)\\n","what":"Implement snapshot commit as a single, atomic operation:\\n\\n  compute EPT + digests\\n    → build snapshot 0.5\).\\n\\nThe commit flow MUST be correct under concurrency, MUST be deterministic given identical canonical state,\\nMUST be idempotent when re-committing an identical state, and MUST record all required manifest fields.\\n\\nRequired manifest content \(minimum\):\\n  - manifest\_schema\_version\\n  - created\_at \(timestamp\)\\n  - repo/profile/policy references:\\n      - policy\_ref \(e.g., provenance\_event\_id\) if present in schema\\n\\nCAS requirements:\\n  - manifest JSON stored as \`kind: manifest\_json\` \(or equivalent\) and indexed in cas\_blobs when healthy.\\n  - CAS write MUST be atomic temp→rename.\\n  - If the same manifest\_digest already exists with identical bytes, treat as success.\\n\\nTransaction boundary:\\n  - The commit operation MUST behave as atomic:\\n      - either \(a\) ledger entry exists AND referenced manifest exists in CAS, or\\n      - \(b\) neither exists \(no partial commit\).\\n  - If CAS write succeeds but ledger append fails, implementation MUST roll back or clean up such that\\n    the system does not observe a ledger entry pointing at a missing manifest.\\n    \(A leftover CAS blob without a ledger reference is acceptable but SHOULD be avoided where feasible.\)\\n\\nAPI surface \(minimum\):\\n  - Engine function: \`snapshot\_commit\(root\_ettle\_id, policy\_ref, profile\_ref, options\) -&gt; snapshot\_id\`\\n  - Options MUST include: expected\_head \(optional\) and dry\_run \(optional\).\\n  - Internal CLI wiring MAY be provided as a thin wrapper, but correctness is in the engine.\\n\\nOut of scope \(for this seed\):\\n  - Snapshot diff algorithm \(manifest-to-manifest diff\)\\n  - Garbage collection / reachability\\n  - Full CLI UX beyond invoking commit\\n\\n\\nManifest content requirements \(CORE frozen fields + additive envelope\):\\n  The snapshot manifest MUST contain, at minimum:\\n    - schema\_version\\n    - facet\_snapshot\_id\\n    - realised\_ettle\_id\\n    - ettle\_version\\n    - created\_at                    # included in manifest bytes; digest is non-deterministic by design\\n    - approver\\n    - policy\_ref\\n    - profile\_ref\\n    - ept                           # ordered EP ids \(the committed EPT\)\\n    - ep\_digests                    # map ep\_id -&gt; digest \(for EPs in ept only\)\\n    - ept\_digest                    # digest of ordered ept structure\\n    - constraints                   # family-agnostic envelope \(see below\)\\n    - coverage                      # coverage metrics object\\n    - exceptions                    # exception list \(may be empty\)\\n    - manifest\_digest               # digest over the exact manifest bytes written to CAS\\n    - semantic\_manifest\_digest      # digest over a canonicalised copy of the manifest with created\_at removed/zeroed\\n\\n  Constraints envelope \(anti-lock-in contract\):\\n    - The manifest MUST contain a top-level \`constraints\` object that is extensible by family.\\n    - The \`constraints\` object MUST be shaped so that ABB→SBB is represented as ONE family, not the whole schema.\\n    - However, to remain compatible with the CORE charter and existing tooling, the \`constraints\` object MUST also\\n      expose the CORE frozen ABB/SBB projections as stable fields.\\n\\n  Required shape \(minimum viable, additive-safe\):\\n    constraints:\\n      declared\_refs: \[\]             # ordered, deterministic list of constraint refs active on the EPT \(may be empty\)\\n      families: {}                  # map family\_name -&gt; {active\_refs, outcomes, evidence, digest} \(may be empty\)\\n      # Frozen ABB→SBB projections \(must exist even if empty\):\\n      applicable\_abb: \[\]            # list of ABB constraint ids\\n      resolved\_sbb: \[\]              # list of resolved SBB constraint ids\\n      resolution\_evidence: \[\]       # opaque evidence records \(predicate matched, selected ids, etc.\)\\n      constraints\_digest: &lt;digest&gt;  # digest over canonicalised constraints envelope \(NOT including created\_at\)\\n\\n  Determinism rules \(binding\):\\n    - \`ept\` order MUST be deterministic \(by EPT computation rules\).\\n    - \`declared\_refs\` order MUST be deterministic:\\n        - primary: family then kind then id \(lexicographic\), unless an explicit ordinal is stored.\\n    - \`families\` keys MUST be ordered deterministically in canonicalisation \(lexicographic\).\\n    - Any list inside \`families\[family\].\*\` MUST be deterministically ordered.\\n","why":"Provide immutable semantic anchors by committing canonical state into an append-only ledger.\\nEnable reliable reproducible diffs and downstream TES generation by persisting a | ep:constraint\_schema\_stubs:0 | ettle:constraint\_schema\_stubs | 0 | 1 | ettle:constraint\_engine\_slice0 | f85cd89a96ec2fe4465c49550d022cd3939e5c36faf4829b5805bc3831f16fd2 | {"how":"Scenarios \(all MUST be implemented as tests; unit/integration; Gherkin is normative\):\\n\\nFeature: Constraint schema stubs and extensibility contract\\n\\n  Background:\\n    Given a repository with SQLite + CAS store initialised\\n    And snapshot commit is already implemented and passing tests\\n\\n  # --- Schema and persistence stubs ---\\n\\n  Scenario: Create a constraint entity with an arbitrary family without code changes\\n    Given a constraint payload JSON with family \\"platform\\" and kind \\"runtime\\"\\n    When I create a constraint with family \\"platform\\" and kind \\"runtime\\"\\n    Then it is stored in canonical state with family \\"platform\\" preserved verbatim\\n    And no validation rejects unknown families\\n\\n  Scenario: Attach multiple constraints to a single EP with stable ordering\\n    Given an EP \\"ep:example:0\\" exists\\n    And two constraints exist \\"c:1\\" and \\"c:2\\"\\n    When I attach \\"c:1\\" with ordinal 0 and \\"c:2\\" with ordinal 1\\n    Then listing EP constraints returns \[\\"c:1\\", \\"c:2\\"\] in ordinal order\\n    And ordinals are immutable \(attempt to reassign fails\)\\n\\n  Scenario: Tombstoning a constraint does not delete historical attachment records\\n    Given constraint \\"c:3\\" is attached to EP \\"ep:example:0\\"\\n    When I tombstone constraint \\"c:3\\"\\n    Then the constraint is excluded from active queries\\n    But historical snapshots that referenced \\"c:3\\" remain readable\\n\\n  # --- Manifest envelope requirements ---\\n\\n  Scenario: Snapshot commit includes a family-agnostic constraints envelope\\n    Given root\_ettle\_id \\"ettle:root\\" exists\\n    And the EPT includes an EP with attached constraints of families \\"pattern\\" and \\"compliance\\"\\n    When I call snapshot\_commit for \\"ettle:root\\"\\n    Then the manifest contains a top-level \\"constraints\\" envelope\\n    And the envelope contains entries for both families\\n    And each entry includes constraint\_id, family, kind, scope, and payload\_digest\\n    And the ordering of constraints in each list is deterministic\\n\\n  Scenario: CORE-required ABB/SBB manifest fields remain present as projection\\n    Given the current closure includes zero ABB/SBB-family constraints\\n    When I call snapshot\_commit\\n    Then manifest fields effective\_abb\_constraints, resolved\_sbb\_selections, and resolution\_evidence exist\\n    And each of those fields is an empty list\\n    And the family-agnostic constraints envelope still exists and is authoritative\\n\\n  Scenario: Unknown constraint families are preserved without interpretation\\n    Given a constraint with family \\"vendor\_ext\\" and payload containing unknown fields\\n    When I call snapshot\_commit\\n    Then the manifest includes that constraint in the constraints envelope\\n    And payload\_digest matches a canonical digest of payload\_json\\n    And no code path attempts to interpret the payload structure\\n\\n  # returned\\n    And one new ledger row is appended\\n    And one manifest blob is written to CAS\\n    And the manifest bytes conform to seed\_snapshot\_commit\_v4.yaml\\n\\n  Scenario: CLI snapshot commit delegates to action:commands\\n    When I invoke \`ettlex snapshot commit --leaf &lt;leaf\_ep\_id&gt;\`\\n    Then the CLI calls action:commands::apply\(Command::SnapshotCommit{leaf\_ep\_id=...}\)\\n    And the CLI does not call store/engine snapshot\_commit directly\\n\\n  Scenario: Store/engine snapshot\_commit remains internal-only\\n    Given I attempt to call store/engine snapshot\_commit from outside the action layer \(in production code\)\\n    Then the build fails due to module visibility OR a lint rule OR a prohibited import boundary\\n    And the policy for this restriction is documented in code comments\\n\\n  # --- Leaf vs root selector alignment ---\\n\\n  Scenario: SnapshotCommit rejects non-leaf EP id\\n    Given EP &lt;ep\_id&gt; exists but is not a leaf under the refinement model\\n    When I call action:commands::apply\(Command::SnapshotCommit{leaf\_ep\_id=&lt;ep\_id&gt;}\)\\n    Then a typed error NotALeaf is returned\\n    And no snapshot is committed\\n\\n  Scenario: SnapshotCommit rejects unknown EP id\\n    When I call action:commands::apply\(Command::SnapshotCommit{leaf\_ep\_id=\\"ep:missing\\"}\)\\n    Then a typed error NotFound is returned\\n    And no snapshot is committed\\n\\n  Scenario: Legacy root selector Ettle &lt;root\_ettle\_id&gt; contains no leaf EPs \(invalid refinement graph\)\\n    When I invoke \`ettlex snapshot commit --root &lt;root\_ettle\_id&gt;\` \(legacy path\)\\n    Then a typed error RootEttleInvalid is returned\\n    And no snapshot is committed\\n\\n  # --- Determinism and invariants ---\\n\\n  Scenario: Snapshot commit output remains deterministic under refactor\\n    Given canonical state is unchanged and leaf\_ep\_id is identical\\n    When I commit snapshot via old internal path in a test harness\\n    And I commit snapshot via action command path\\n    Then semantic\_manifest\_digest is identical\\n    And ept\_digest is identical\\n    And manifest bytes are identical except for created\_at and manifest\_digest\\n\\n  Scenario: Snapshot commit preserves created\_at non-determinism rule\\n    Given created\_at is included in manifest bytes\\n    When I commit twice with identical state\\n    Then manifest\_digest differs\\n    And semantic\_manifest\_digest is identical\\n\\n  Scenario: No extra mutation occurs during commit\\n    When I call Command::SnapshotCommit\\n    Then no Ettle, EP, link, or constraint rows are modified\\n    And only the ledger and CAS are written\\n\\n  # --- Policy and error taxonomy propagation ---\\n\\n  Scenario: Policy gating is enforced in action layer\\n    Given a policy profile denies snapshot commit for this leaf\\n    When I call Command::SnapshotCommit\\n    Then a typed error PolicyDenied is returned\\n    And no ledger row is appended\\n    And no CAS write occurs\\n\\n returned\\n    And the error includes a stable error\_code\\n    And no partial ledger write remains \(transactional safety\)\\n\\n  Scenario: EPT ambiguity fails fast with typed error\\n    Given the refinement graph is ambiguous under EPT algorithm\\n    When I call Command::SnapshotCommit\\n    Then a typed error EptAmbiguous is returned\\n    And no snapshot is committed\\n\\n  # --- Boundary conditions ---\\n\\n  Scenario: Snapshot commit is idempotent only by explicit option\\n    Given a snapshot with identical semantic\_manifest\_digest already exists\\n    When I call Command::SnapshotCommit without options\\n    Then a new snapshot is still committed \(append-only\)\\n    And the system does not auto-deduplicate\\n    When I call Command::SnapshotCommit with option allow\_dedup=true\\n    Then the system MAY return existing snapshot\_id\\n    And MUST record an event describing reuse \(if reuse occurs\)\\n\\n  Scenario: Snapshot commit handles large configured limits","what":"Refactor snapshot\_commit so that:\\n\\n1\) Canonical mutation ingress\\n   - A new Action Command MUST exist:\\n       Command::SnapshotCommit { leaf\_ep\_id, policy\_ref?, profile\_ref?, options? }\\n   - The ONLY supported way to commit a snapshot in production code MUST be via action:commands::apply\\n     with Command::SnapshotCommit.\\n   - Engine/store snapshot\_commit functions MAY remain internal, but MUST be called only from the action\\n     command implementation, and MUST NOT encode semantic rules.\\n\\n1.1\) Leaf-scoped selector \(terminology alignment\)\\n   - SnapshotCommit MUST be leaf-scoped:\\n       \* The primary selector MUST be leaf\_ep\_id \(an EP id\).\\n       \* root\_ettle\_id MUST NOT be the primary commit selector.\\n   - Definition of \\"leaf under the refinement model\\":\\n       \* A leaf EP is an EP that has no child Ettle \(i.e., it is not linked to any child\_ettle\_id\).\\n       \* Leaf status is determined structurally \(no outgoing refine-to-child edge\),\\n         not by ordinal position within its Ettle.\\n       \* If an Ettle contains multiple EPs, some with children and some without,\\n         only those EPs without child Ettles qualify as valid leaf\_ep\_id values.\\n   - The action layer MUST derive root\_ettle\_id internally \(via EP→Ettle membership\) for bookkeeping,\\n     provenance, and manifest fields that require it.\\n   - If any legacy interface accepts root\_ettle\_id \(e.g., CLI flag or internal API\), it MUST resolve to\\n     exactly one leaf EP deterministically or fail with a typed error.\\n     \* Deterministic resolution rule \(if legacy root is supported\):\\n         - If the Ettle has exactly one leaf EP under the refinement model, resolve to that leaf.\\n         - Otherwise fail with RootEttleAmbiguous \(do NOT pick arbitrarily\).\\n\\n2\) Stable semantics\\n   - The committed manifest content MUST remain compliant with seed\_snapshot\_commit\_v4.yaml.\\n writes\\n       \* CAS blob writes\\n       \* returning low-level IO errors\\n\\n4\) Compatibility\\n   - Existing CLI code MUST be re-wired to call the action command rather than calling engine/store directly.\\n   - No external interface \(seed import/export, snapshot identifiers\) changes are permitted in this refactor.\\n   - If the CLI already supports a root-based flag, it MAY continue to exist but MUST behave as legacy:\\n       \* it resolves root→leaf deterministically as per 1.1, or fails with RootEttleAmbiguous.","why":"Snapshot commit is a canonical mutation: it additive\):\\n  1\) decisions\\n     - decision\_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY\\n     - title TEXT NOT NULL\\n     - status TEXT NOT NULL                  # proposed\|accepted\|superseded\|rejected \(open set allowed\)\\n     - decision\_text TEXT NOT NULL\\n     - rationale TEXT NOT NULL\\n     - alternatives\_text TEXT NULL\\n     - consequences\_text TEXT NULL\\n     - evidence\_kind TEXT NOT NULL           # none\|excerpt\|capture\|file \(open set allowed\)\\n     - evidence\_excerpt TEXT NULL            # portable short excerpt \(recommended for 'excerpt' and 'capture'\)\\n     - evidence\_capture\_id TEXT NULL         # optional FK into decision\_evidence\_items when used\\n     - evidence\_file\_path TEXT NULL          # optional repo-relative path when used \(portable\)\\n     - evidence\_hash TEXT NULL               # sha256 over canonical evidence content when applicable\\n     - created\_at TEXT NOT NULL\\n     - updated\_at TEXT NOT NULL\\n     - tombstoned\_at TEXT NULL               # tombstone, optional but recommended\\n\\n  2\) decision\_evidence\_items \(OPTIONAL but RECOMMENDED; names are normative within the action layer\):\\n  - DecisionCreate\(decision\_id?, title, status?, decision\_text, rationale,\\n                   alternatives\_text?, consequences\_text?,\\n                   evidence\_kind, evidence\_excerpt?, evidence\_capture\_content?, evidence\_file\_path?\)\\n      -&gt; \(\)\\n\\n  - DecisionTombstone\(decision\_id\) -&gt; \(\)\\n    Notes:\\n      - Tombstoning MUST NOT delete rows; it marks tombstoned\_at and prevents new links by default.\\n\\n  - DecisionLink\(decision\_id, target\_kind, target\_id, relation\_kind, ordinal?\) -&gt; new, relation\_kind=\\"supersedes\\"\) or equivalent.\\n      - Supersede MUST NOT implicitly tombstone the old decision.\\n\\nRequired action:queries \(minimum; read-only\):\\n  - decision.get\(decision\_id\) -&gt; ordered list\\n  - ept.compute\_decision\_context\(leaf\_ep\_id, status\_filter?, relation\_filter?\)\\n      -&gt; { direct\_by\_ep: {ep\_id: \[decisions...\]}, inherited\_for\_leaf: \[decisions...\] }\\n    Notes:\\n      - This query MUST use the canonical refinement graph / EPT projection for ancestor enumeration.\\n      - This query is read-only and MUST be deterministic.\\n\\nRead/Render integration contract \(binding; via action:queries\):\\n  - Existing EP and EPT read queries \(if present\) MUST be able to optionally include decision summaries.\\n  - Implementations MAY add flags like include\_decisions/include\_ancestor\_decisions to ep.get / ept.compute views.\\n  - If such flags are added, they MUST call the decision queries above and MUST NOT introduce bespoke store reads.\\n\\nOut of scope \(explicitly deferred\):\\n  - Automatic extraction from transcripts without user/agent-curated capture content\\n  - Policy gating \(e.g. \\"accepted decision required to commit\\"\)\\n  - Decision evaluation semantics \(e.g. UngroundedDecision\) and evidence workflows\\n  - Snapshot manifest projection of decisions and decision diffs","why":"Human/AI authoring and refinement produces binding design decisions before and during Ettle/EP authoring.\\nIf those decisions are not captured as first-class canonical artefacts, the system loses provenance and\\ngovernance traceability; rationale becomes scattered across chat logs \(non-portable\) or embedded ad hoc\\nin EP.HOW prose \(hard to diff, hard to audit\).\\n\\nThis seed introduces the minimal canonical persistence and query-friendly linkage stubs needed so that:\\n  - MCP \(and later CLI/UI\) can capture decisions at the moment they are made,\\n  - decisions can be viewed in context with EPs and the EPT projection,\\n  - later work can add policy gates, evidence workflows, and snapshot projections without schema churn.\\n\\nThis seed is intentionally non-load-bearing for snapshot semantics:\\n  - Decisions are canonical governance artefacts, not part of snapshot semantic closure in this tier.\\n  - Snapshot manifests and semantic\_manifest\_digest MUST remain unaffected by decision content/links."} | 0 | 1771885507 | 1771885507 | null | ettle:decision\_schema\_stubs | Design Decision Schema Stubs \(canonical decisions + EP/Ettle linkage; All executable scenarios live in leaf children.","what":"This Ettle is intentionally NON-LEAF and therefore NON-IMPLEMENTABLE directly.\\n\\nContract \(MUST be satisfied by child implementations\):\\n\\n1\) Canonical profile identity and immutability\\n   - A Profile is addressable by a stable profile\_ref string of the form:\\n       profile/&lt;profile\_id&gt;@&lt;version&gt;\\n   - profile\_id MUST be a non-empty identifier with a restricted character set to avoid ambiguity and\\n     path injection \(implementation-defined, but MUST be deterministic and documented\).\\n   - version MUST be a non-negative integer in Phase 1.\\n   - Each profile version MUST be immutable once created. Any update MUST create a new version.\\n\\n2\) Deterministic profile resolution\\n   - Any API accepting profile\_ref MUST resolve to a stored profile version deterministically.\\n   - If profile\_ref is omitted, resolution MUST follow a deterministic defaulting rule.\\n\\n3\) Minimal governance knobs \(normative semantics\)\\n   - Profiles MUST provide, at minimum:\\n       ambiguity\_policy: fail\_fast \| route\_for\_approval \| choose\_deterministic\\n       approval\_routing: { required: bool, channel: string }\\n       determinism\_mode: strict \| permissive\\n   - If ambiguity\_policy=route\_for\_approval then approval\_routing.required MUST be true.\\n\\n4\) Consumers accept resolved Profile objects\\n   - Downstream components \(predicate evaluator, snapshot commit policy, etc.\) MUST accept a resolved\\n     Profile object \(structured\) and MUST NOT treat profile\_ref as an opaque string.\\n   - Resolved Profile objects MUST contain:\\n       \* profile\_ref\\n       \* profile\_digest\\n       \* parsed payload \(minimal knobs at least\)\\n       \* optional metadata \(created\_at, source\) if available\\n\\n5\) route\_for\_approval produces durable, queryable approval requests\\n   - When profile requires route\_for\_approval, the system MUST create a durable approval request object\\n     and return an approval\_token.\\n   - Approval requests MUST be queryable through read surfaces \(queries\) for later workflow integration.\\n   - Approval requests MUST include stable comparison data \(semantic\_request\_digest\) so workflows can deduplicate.\\n\\n6\) CAS + SQLite discipline\\n   - Canonical payload bytes for Profiles and Approval Requests MUST be stored in CAS and referenced by digest.\\n   - SQLite provides indexes and lookups; missing indexes MUST NOT prevent correctness if CAS is present\\n     \(non-load-bearing principle\), but MUST be populated when healthy.\\n   - CAS layout MUST follow: cas/&lt;shard&gt;/&lt;digest&gt;.json, with atomic temp-&gt;rename writes.\\n\\n7\) Determinism commitments\\n   - For the same semantic input, the same canonical bytes MUST be produced \(except where explicitly allowed,\\n     e.g., created\_at included in request\_digest but excluded from semantic\_request\_digest\).\\n   - Any determinism instability MUST raise DeterminismViolation in strict mode.","why":"Profiles are the “governance dial” for EttleX: they parameterise how ambiguity, approval routing,\\nand safety/guardrail constraints are handled without forking core algorithms.\\n\\nPhase 1 requires profile handling to be real \(not merely a string carried into manifests\), because:\\n  - the Minimal Constraint Predicate Evaluator MUST be able to route ambiguity via profile rules, and\\n  - snapshot commit MUST be policy/profile-governed and fail fast unless explicitly routed under profile.\\n\\nIn the refinement model, this node is an abstract parent and exists to anchor implementable leaf children\\nthat provide:\\n  - profile persistence + resolution + versioning \(Profiles Core\)\\n  - profile-governed constraint predicate evaluation \(Constraint Predicates\)\\n  - profile authoring commands + approval routing primitives \(Profiles Actions\)\\n\\nThis Ettle also exists to keep the semantics \*inside the engine\* rather than in the MCP or CLI transports.\\nMCP/CLI MUST remain thin adapters over the same engine Commands/Queries."} | 0 | 1772195064 | 1772195064 | null | ettle:profiles | Profiles — Governance Dial \(Abstract Parent\) | null | 0 | 2026-02-27T12:24:24Z | 2026-02-27T12:24:24Z | {"data":{}} | null |  |  |  | null | null | 2026-03-22T19:40:28.278549+00:00 |

rules in the action command layer \(Command::SnapshotCommit\),\\nfocusing on fail-fast behaviour and route\_for\_approval.\\n\\nDependencies \(MUST exist or be stubbed behind interfaces as described\):\\n  - snapshot commit pipeline exists \(ettle:snapshot\_commit end-to-end\)\\n  - profile resolution exists \(ettle:profiles\_core\)\\n  - approval routing primitives exist \(ettle:profiles\_actions\)\\n  - constraint predicate evaluator exists \(ettle:constraint\_predicates\)\\n  - a policy hook exists \(may be minimal/opaque in Phase 1 but MUST be testable\)\\n\\n1\) Inputs \(normative\)\\n   - leaf\_ep\_id \(primary selector; required\)\\n   - policy\_ref \(optional string; deterministic defaulting may apply\)\\n   - profile\_ref \(optional string; deterministic defaulting per Profiles Core\)\\n   - options:\\n       \* expected\_head \(optional\)\\n       \* dry\_run \(bool\)\\n       \* other existing commit options\\n\\n  Expected head gating \(normative; optimistic concurrency\):\\n    - During snapshot\_commit, the system MUST resolve the commit target realised\_ettle\_id prior to durable writes.\\n      \(The realised\_ettle\_id is the lineage key that the commit will append to.\)\\n    - Head definition \(binding\): Head = the manifest\_digest of the latest committed snapshot for a given realised\_ettle\_id.\\n      If no prior snapshot exists for the realised\_ettle\_id, Head is None.\\n    - If options.expected\_head is provided:\\n        \* The system MUST read head\_before \(as defined above\) at the start of the commit.\\n        \* If head\_before is None, the commit MUST fail with HeadMismatch.\\n        \* If head\_before is Some\(H\) and expected\_head != H, the commit MUST fail with HeadMismatch.\\n        \* On HeadMismatch, no durable writes of any kind may occur \(no ledger rows, no facet snapshots, no approvals\).\\n    - If options.expected\_head is not provided:\\n        \* No head gating is performed.\\n    - On successful commit, head\_after MUST equal the manifest\_digest of the newly committed manifest.\\n\\n\\n2\) Policy hook \(Phase 1 minimum, normative\)\\n   - Before any commit work that performs durable writes, the system MUST evaluate an allow/deny hook:\\n       policy\_check\(policy\_ref, profile\_ref, leaf\_ep\_id, context?\) -&gt; allow\|deny\\n   - If denied:\\n       \* return typed error PolicyDenied\\n       \* perform NO manifest CAS writes and NO facet\_snapshots ledger append\\n       \* perform NO approval routing \(PolicyDenied is a hard stop\)\\n\\n3\) Selector validity and structural gating \(normative\)\\n   - If leaf\_ep\_id does not exist: return NotFound and perform no writes.\\n   - If leaf\_ep\_id exists but is not a leaf under the refinement model: return NotALeaf and perform no writes.\\n   - If legacy root selector path exists:\\n       \* if it resolves to multiple leaves: RootEttleAmbiguous \(NOT waivable\) and no writes\\n       \* if it resolves to zero leaves: RootEttleInvalid and no writes\\n\\n4\) EPT gating and determinism \(normative\)\\n   - EPT computation MUST be performed deterministically.\\n   - If EPT is ambiguous: return EptAmbiguous \(NOT waivable\) and no writes.\\n   - If determinism violation is detected in EPT ordering or traversal: return DeterminismViolation \(NOT waivable\) and no writes.\\n\\n5\) Constraint resolution gating \(normative\)\\n   - Snapshot commit MUST obtain constraint\_resolution via the predicate evaluator \(or equivalent\), even if the result is empty.\\n   - If predicate evaluator produces:\\n       a\) NoMatch or Selected: commit may proceed\\n       b\) AmbiguousSelection:\\n            - if profile.ambiguity\_policy = fail\_fast:\\n                return AmbiguousSelection error \(no writes; no approval request\)\\n            - if profile.ambiguity\_policy = choose\_deterministic:\\n                commit proceeds using the chosen candidate; the chosen candidate MUST be recorded in manifest.constraint\_resolution\\n            - if profile.ambiguity\_policy = route\_for\_approval:\\n                \* MUST call ApprovalRouter.route\_approval\_request with kind=snapshot\_commit \(preferred\) OR constraint\_ambiguity,\\n                  but reason\_code MUST be AmbiguousSelection\\n                \* MUST return RoutedForApproval{approval\_token, reason\_code, candidate\_set}\\n                \* MUST perform NO manifest CAS write and NO ledger append \(facet\_snapshots\)\\n                \* MUST be testable via Query::ApprovalGet\(approval\_token\)\\n            - if route\_for\_approval but router unavailable: return ApprovalRoutingUnavailable and no writes\\n\\n6\) Waivable vs non-waivable ambiguity set \(normative\)\\n   - Waivable \(may route\_for\_approval\):\\n       \* constraint candidate ambiguity \(AmbiguousSelection\)\\n   - NOT waivable \(MUST fail fast regardless of profile\):\\n       \* RootEttleAmbiguous\\n       \* EptAmbiguous\\n       \* DeterminismViolation\\n\\n7\) dry\_run semantics \(normative\)\\n   - dry\_run=true MUST perform no durable writes regardless of ambiguity or success.\\n   - dry\_run=true MUST NOT create approval requests \(because it is not a real workflow step\).\\n   - dry\_run may return computed data \(e.g., would-be digests\), but MUST document which fields are stable.\\n\\n8\) Transaction / write invariants \(normative\)\\n   - On any failure \(typed error\), there MUST be:\\n       \* no facet\_snapshots row appended\\n       \* no manifest CAS write considered committed output of the operation\\n       \* no cas\_blobs upsert related to manifest\\n   - On RoutedForApproval, the ONLY permitted durable writes are:\\n       \* approval request persistence \(CAS + approval\_requests index/provenance\)\\n     and there MUST be:\\n       \* no facet\_snapshots row appended\\n       \* no manifest CAS write\\n       \* no cas\_blobs upsert for manifest\\n\\n9\) Created\_at and semantic digests \(normative\)\\n   - The manifest bytes include created\_at.\\n   - Therefore, manifest\_digest may vary between otherwise identical commits.\\n   - The system MUST compute semantic\_manifest\_digest excluding created\_at and MUST record it.\\n   - semantic\_manifest\_digest MUST be used for comparisons and determinism checks where appropriate\\n     \(e.g., test harness comparing two manifests for semantic equivalence\).\\n\\n10\) Output types \(normative\)\\n   - Success: SnapshotCommitted{snapshot\_id, manifest\_digest, semantic\_manifest\_digest, head\_after, ...}\\n   - head\_after \(binding\): MUST equal the manifest\_digest of the newly committed manifest \(the new Head of the realised\_ettle\_id lineage\).\\n      For clarity: the command MAY compute and use head\_before for expected\_head gating, but only head\_after is required to be returned.\\n    \\n   - Routed: RoutedForApproval{approval\_token, reason\_code, candidate\_set}\\n   - Failure: typed errors:\\n       NotFound, NotALeaf, RootEttleAmbiguous, RootEttleInvalid,\\n       EptAmbiguous, DeterminismViolation,\\n       AmbiguousSelection, ApprovalRoutingUnavailable,\\n       PolicyDenied, HeadMismatch, ProfileNotFound, ...","why":"Snapshot commit is a canonical mutation that creates durable semantic anchors. MUST NOT call store/engine mutation functions directly.\\n\\n  C\) Determinism and canonicalisation\\n     - MCP outputs MUST be deterministic for identical action-layer outputs.\\n     - Where         - action layer policy/profile hooks.\\n     - MCP MUST allow policy\_ref and profile\_ref to be passed for operations that support them\\n       \(e.g. SnapshotCommit\).\\n\\n  E\) Security and operational posture \(Phase 1/early Phase 2\)\\n     - MCP MUST support a minimal dev auth mode \(e.g. allowlist token\) with explicit “auth disabled” configuration.\\n     - No complex deterministic\)\\n\\n\\nAdditional Phase 1 profile/approval requirements \(binding\):\\n\\n  G\) Profile authoring and approval routing must be reachable via MCP without seeds\\n     - MCP MUST expose MUST remain in action layer.\\n\\nResponse shaping rules \(binding\):\\n  - ettlex.apply MUST return a stable envelope. If the underlying command returns a union result, MCP MUST preserve\\n    the union tag in a stable way \(e.g., { result: { tag: \\"SnapshotCommitted\\", ... } }\).\\n  - RoutedForApproval is a first-class success result and MUST be returned as:\\n      { new\_state\_version, result: { tag: \\"RoutedForApproval\\", approval\_token, reason\_code?, candidate\_set? } }\\n    \(field names must match action DTOs; MCP MUST NOT rename domain fields\).\\nError mapping contract \(binding\):\\n  - MCP MUST surface action-layer typed errors as stable tool errors:\\n      { error\_code, message, details?, correlation\_id }\\n  - Error codes MUST be stable and testable. EpCreate — ep\_id field removed from command schema\\n   - The EpCreate command MUST NOT accept an ep\_id field.\\n   - The store MUST always generate a ULID for new EP identity.\\n   - If an ep\_id field is present in the EpCreate payload the command MUST be rejected with error code InvalidInput before any mutation occurs.\\n   - The generated ep\_id MUST be returned in the command result.\\n\\n3. PolicyCreate — added to Apply command vocabulary\\n   - A new Apply command MUST exist: PolicyCreate { policy\_ref: String, text: String }\\n   - policy\_ref is the caller-supplied stable semantic reference \(e.g. codegen\_handoff@1\). It is NOT store-generated.\\n   - text is the full policy body including HANDOFF markers.\\n   - The store MUST persist the policy as a file-backed document addressable by policy\_ref.\\n   - PolicyCreate MUST fail with PolicyConflict if a policy with the same policy\_ref already exists. No silent overwrite is permitted.\\n   - PolicyCreate MUST fail with InvalidInput if text is empty.\\n   - PolicyCreate MUST fail with InvalidInput if policy\_ref is empty or malformed.\\n   - After successful PolicyCreate, the policy MUST be immediately retrievable via policy.get\(policy\_ref\).\\n   - PolicyCreate MUST be atomic: either the policy is persisted and retrievable, or it is not. Partial persistence is not permitted.\\n   - PolicyCreate MUST increment state\_version by exactly 1 on success.\\n\\n4. Identity vs reference invariant \(binding across all commands\)\\n   - Entity identity fields \(ettle\_id, ep\_id\) MUST always be store-generated ULIDs.\\n   - Semantic reference fields \(policy\_ref, profile\_ref\) MUST be caller-supplied stable strings.\\n   - No command MUST silently discard a supplied field; presence of a disallowed field MUST be rejected with InvalidInput.","why":"EttleCreate and EpCreate both accept caller-supplied identity fields \(ettle\_id and ep\_id\) but silently ignore them, always generating ULIDs. This is a silent contract violation: callers cannot control identity through the Apply surface, but the schema implies they can.\\n\\nThe seed import path that motivated caller-supplied IDs is a throwaway bootstrapping mechanism being phased out in favour of MCP/CLI/UI. There is no production use case for caller-supplied entity IDs through Apply commands. The store owns identity, always.\\n\\nSeparately, PolicyCreate is absent from the Apply command vocabulary. Policies are currently file-backed only. This creates a bootstrapping deadlock: SnapshotCommit requires a policy\_ref, but the MCP cannot create policies. PolicyCreate must be added as a first-class Apply command.\\n\\nNote on identity vs reference: policy\_ref is a stable semantic reference \(e.g. codegen\_handoff@1\), not a database primary key. Caller-supplied policy\_ref in PolicyCreate is correct and is the intended exception to the ULID-only rule. The distinction is: entity identity \(Ettle, EP\) is always store-generated; semantic references \(policy\_ref, profile\_ref\) are caller-supplied stable strings.\\n\\nNon-goals: changing ULID generation; altering other command signatures; policy enforcement semantics."} | 0 | 1772893390 | 1772893390 | null | ettle:store | Storage Spine \(SQLite + CAS + Seed Import\) | ettle:root | 0 | 2026-02-22T20:18:05Z | 2026-02-22T20:18:05Z | {"data":{}} | ep:root:1 |  |  |  | null | null | 2026-03-22T19:40:13.943607+00:00 |

The sequence failed because no policy existed in the store and PolicyCreate was absent from the command vocabulary. Even after ProfileCreate was added, SnapshotCommit remained unreachable.\\n\\nThis EP makes the optionality of policy\_ref binding and specifies the deterministic defaulting behaviour when it is omitted. An Ettle is the complete reasoning space for a deliberate aim — it contains the original aim, all refinements, all explored branches, all rejected options. The refinement tree is internal to it. determinism — CRUD outputs are not digest-compared here.\\n  # N/A: Concurrency beyond OCC — SQLite serialises writes.","what":"## 1. Schema changes — single migration file \(012\)\\n\\nThe project uses rusqlite 0.29 with the \`bundled\` feature, which compiles SQLite 3.43.x.\\nThis version fully supports ALTER TABLE RENAME COLUMN \(since 3.25.0\) and DROP COLUMN\\n\(since 3.35.0\). A clean single migration is therefore correct and preferred.\\n\\n### 1.1 Migration file\\n\\nFile: migrations/012\_structural\_model\_update.sql\\n\\nThis migration MUST:\\n  - Rename eps.ettle\_id to eps.containing\_ettle.\\n  - Rename ettles.parent\_id to ettles.parent\_ettle\_id.\\n  - Drop ettles.parent\_ep\_id \(added in migration 009; conflated the two link trees\).\\n  - Drop eps.child\_ettle\_id \(replaced by eps.parent\_ep\_id in the new model\).\\n  - Drop eps.content\_digest and eps.content\_inline \(content is carried in the\\n    existing content JSON field; dual-storage pattern is removed\).\\n  - Add eps.parent\_ep\_id TEXT REFERENCES eps\(id\) \(nullable; new cross-Ettle link\).\\n  - Drop index idx\_eps\_ettle\_id \(references old column name\).\\n  - Drop index idx\_ettles\_parent\_id \(references old column name\).\\n  - Create index idx\_eps\_containing\_ettle ON eps\(containing\_ettle\).\\n  - Create index idx\_eps\_containing\_ettle\_ordinal ON eps\(containing\_ettle, ordinal\).\\n  - Create index idx\_ettles\_parent\_ettle\_id ON ettles\(parent\_ettle\_id\).\\n  - Create index idx\_eps\_parent\_ep\_id ON eps\(parent\_ep\_id\).\\n\\neps.parent\_ep\_id starts as NULL for all existing rows. The DB repair that populates\\nexisting parent\_ep\_id values is performed via EpUpdate commands once the command\\nlayer is available in this Ettle; no backfill SQL is needed.\\n\\nComment block MUST be included:\\n  -- Migration 012: Structural model update.\\n  -- Renames ettle\_id-&gt;containing\_ettle, parent\_id-&gt;parent\_ettle\_id.\\n  -- Drops child\_ettle\_id, parent\_ep\_id \(on ettles\), content\_digest, content\_inline.\\n  -- Adds eps.parent\_ep\_id \(cross-Ettle EP refinement link\).\\n  -- Requires rusqlite bundled \(SQLite &gt;= 3.35.0 for DROP COLUMN\).\\n  -- See ettle:019ccf15-e2b1-7e33-9794-bf2cf0704178 EP0 for full specification.\\n\\n### 1.2 UNIQUE constraint\\n\\nThe existing UNIQUE \(ettle\_id, ordinal\) constraint on eps must be recreated as\\nUNIQUE \(containing\_ettle, ordinal\) after the rename. SQLite requires a table\\nrecreation to alter constraints; the migration MUST handle this via the\\ncreate-new-table / copy / drop-old / rename pattern if the rename alone does not\\npreserve the constraint name correctly. The agent MUST verify the constraint is\\npresent and correctly named after migration.\\n\\n## 2. Domain type updates \(ettlex-core-types\)\\n\\n  - EttleRecord MUST reflect: id, title, parent\_ettle\_id \(Option&lt;String&gt;\), deleted,\\n    created\_at, updated\_at, metadata.\\n    Old fields parent\_id and parent\_ep\_id MUST NOT appear.\\n  - EpRecord MUST reflect: id, containing\_ettle \(String\), ordinal, title \(Option&lt;String&gt;\),\\n    normative, content \(JSON\), digest \(Option&lt;String&gt;\), parent\_ep\_id \(Option&lt;String&gt;\),\\n    deleted, created\_at, updated\_at.\\n    Old fields ettle\_id, child\_ettle\_id, content\_digest, content\_inline MUST NOT appear.\\n  - Update EttleCreateCommand: add parent\_ettle\_id: Option&lt;String&gt;.\\n  - Update EttleUpdateCommand: add parent\_ettle\_id: Option&lt;Option&lt;String&gt;&gt;\\n    \(outer Option = field present in request; inner Option = nullable value\).\\n  - Add EttleTombstoneCommand { ettle\_id: String }.\\n  - Update EpCreateCommand: containing\_ettle replaces ettle\_id; add parent\_ep\_id: Option&lt;String&gt;.\\n  - Update EpUpdateCommand: add parent\_ep\_id: Option&lt;Option&lt;String&gt;&gt;.\\n  - Add EpTombstoneCommand { ep\_id: String }.\\n  - Add error variants:\\n    SameEttleParentLink, EttleTreeInconsistency, SelfReferentialEttle,\\n    EttleCycleDetected, EpCycleDetected, DeletedEttle, DeletedEp,\\n    AlreadyDeleted, HasActiveChildren, HasActiveEps, RefinementIntegrityViolation.\\n\\n## 3. Integrity constraints \(enforced in engine/action layer, not DB triggers\)\\n\\n  IC-1: eps.parent\_ep\_id MUST reference an EP whose containing\_ettle differs from\\n        the referencing EP's containing\_ettle. Same-Ettle parent links MUST be\\n        rejected with typed error SameEttleParentLink.\\n\\n  IC-2: If EP B has parent\_ep\_id pointing to EP A \(in Ettle X\), then B's\\n        containing\_ettle \(Ettle Y\) MUST have parent\_ettle\_id = X. If this consistency\\n        is violated the command MUST fail with typed error EttleTreeInconsistency.\\n\\n  IC-3: An EP MUST have at most one parent EP \(parent\_ep\_id is a single nullable\\n        column; strict tree enforced structurally\).\\n\\n  IC-4: ettles.parent\_ettle\_id MUST NOT reference the Ettle itself \(no self-loops\).\\n        Violation MUST be rejected with typed error SelfReferentialEttle.\\n\\n  IC-5: A cycle in parent\_ettle\_id links MUST be detected and rejected with typed\\n        error EttleCycleDetected.\\n\\n  IC-6: A cycle in parent\_ep\_id links MUST be detected and rejected with typed error\\n        EpCycleDetected.\\n\\n## 4. Command vocabulary changes \(action layer\)\\n\\nAll commands MUST flow through action:commands::apply. No store/engine mutation\\nfunctions MAY be called directly from CLI or MCP.\\n\\n### 4.1 EttleCreate\\n  Input fields:\\n    - title \(required, non-empty string\)\\n    - parent\_ettle\_id \(optional; if supplied, referenced Ettle MUST exist and MUST NOT be deleted\)\\n    - metadata \(optional JSON\)\\n  Output: { ettle\_id, new\_state\_version }\\n  Invariants:\\n    - Generated ettle\_id MUST be stable \(ULIDv7 or equivalent\).\\n    - If parent\_ettle\_id is supplied and does not exist: typed error NotFound.\\n    - If parent\_ettle\_id is supplied and is deleted: typed error DeletedEttle.\\n\\n### 4.2 EttleUpdate\\n  Input fields:\\n    - ettle\_id \(required\)\\n    - title \(optional; if supplied replaces existing title; MUST be non-empty\)\\n    - parent\_ettle\_id \(optional; if supplied replaces existing parent; null clears the parent\)\\n    - metadata \(optional; if supplied replaces existing metadata\)\\n  Output: { new\_state\_version }\\n  Invariants:\\n    - If ettle\_id does not exist: typed error NotFound.\\n    - If ettle\_id is deleted: typed error DeletedEttle.\\n    - If new parent\_ettle\_id would create a cycle: typed error EttleCycleDetected.\\n    - IC-4 applies: self-referential parent rejected with SelfReferentialEttle.\\n    - Updating parent\_ettle\_id does NOT implicitly update any EP parent\_ep\_id fields.\\n      Tree consistency \(IC-2\) is the responsibility of the caller.\\n\\n### 4.3 EttleTombstone\\n  Input fields:\\n    - ettle\_id \(required\)\\n  Output: { new\_state\_version }\\n  Invariants:\\n    - Sets deleted = 1 and updated\_at; does NOT delete rows \(append-only\).\\n    - If ettle\_id does not exist: typed error NotFound.\\n    - If already tombstoned: typed error AlreadyDeleted.\\n    - Tombstoning an Ettle that has non-deleted child Ettles \(via parent\_ettle\_id\)\\n      MUST be rejected with typed error HasActiveChildren.\\n    - Tombstoning an Ettle that contains non-deleted EPs MUST be rejected with\\n      typed error HasActiveEps.\\n\\n### 4.4 EpCreate\\n  Input fields:\\n    - ettle\_id \(required; stored as containing\_ettle; referenced Ettle MUST exist and not be deleted\)\\n    - ordinal \(required; integer &gt;= 0; MUST be unique within the Ettle\)\\n    - normative \(required; boolean\)\\n    - title \(optional string\)\\n    - why, what, how \(optional strings; stored as JSON in content field\)\\n    - parent\_ep\_id \(optional; if supplied IC-1 and IC-2 MUST be enforced\)\\n  Output: { ep\_id, new\_state\_version }\\n  Invariants:\\n    - Generated ep\_id MUST be stable \(ULIDv7 or equivalent\).\\n    - Ordinal MUST be unique within the Ettle; duplicate rejected with OrdinalConflict.\\n    - If parent\_ep\_id does not exist: typed error NotFound.\\n    - If parent\_ep\_id is deleted: typed error DeletedEp.\\n    - IC-1: same-Ettle parent rejected with SameEttleParentLink.\\n    - IC-2: Ettle tree consistency enforced; violation rejected with EttleTreeInconsistency.\\n    - IC-6: cycle detection on parent\_ep\_id; rejected with EpCycleDetected.\\n\\n### 4.5 EpUpdate\\n  Input fields:\\n    - ep\_id \(required\)\\n    - title \(optional; replaces existing\)\\n    - why, what, how \(optional strings; each replaces its respective field in content JSON\)\\n    - normative \(optional; replaces existing\)\\n    - parent\_ep\_id \(optional; replaces existing parent; null clears the parent link\)\\n  Output: { new\_state\_version }\\n  Invariants:\\n    - If ep\_id does not exist: typed error NotFound.\\n    - If ep\_id is deleted: typed error DeletedEp.\\n    - IC-1, IC-2, IC-6 apply when parent\_ep\_id is being set or changed.\\n    - Updating parent\_ep\_id MUST NOT implicitly update ettles.parent\_ettle\_id.\\n      Ettle tree consistency \(IC-2\) is the responsibility of the caller.\\n\\n### 4.6 EpTombstone\\n  Input fields:\\n    - ep\_id \(required\)\\n  Output: { new\_state\_version }\\n  Invariants:\\n    - Sets deleted = 1 and updated\_at; does NOT delete rows.\\n    - If ep\_id does not exist: typed error NotFound.\\n    - If already tombstoned: typed error AlreadyDeleted.\\n    - Tombstoning an EP that has child EPs \(via parent\_ep\_id on other EPs\) MUST be\\n      rejected with typed error HasActiveChildren.\\n\\n## 5. Query surface changes \(action:queries\)\\n\\n  - ettle.get\(ettle\_id\) MUST return: id, title, parent\_ettle\_id, deleted, created\_at,\\n    updated\_at, metadata, and the list of non-deleted EP ids belonging to the Ettle\\n    \(via containing\_ettle lookup\). Does NOT return parent\_id or parent\_ep\_id.\\n  - ep.get\(ep\_id\) MUST return: id, containing\_ettle, ordinal, title, normative,\\n    why, what, how, digest, parent\_ep\_id, deleted, created\_at, updated\_at.\\n    Does NOT return ettle\_id, child\_ettle\_id, content\_digest, content\_inline.\\n  - ep.list\_children\(ep\_id\) MUST return EPs where parent\_ep\_id = ep\_id \(direct\\n    children only; non-deleted by default; include\_deleted option available\).\\n  - ep.list\_parents\(ep\_id\) MUST return the single parent EP via parent\_ep\_id on this\\n    EP, or empty if root. If the data is corrupt and multiple parents are somehow\\n    present \(impossible under new schema but guarded for safety\), MUST return\\n    RefinementIntegrityViolation.\\n  - ettle.list\_children\(ettle\_id\) MUST return Ettles where parent\_ettle\_id = ettle\_id.\\n  - ettle.list\_parents\(ettle\_id\) MUST return the single parent Ettle via parent\_ettle\_id,\\n    or empty if root.\\n  - All existing query tools that previously referenced ettle\_id on EPs MUST be updated\\n    to reference containing\_ettle.\\n  - All existing query tools that previously referenced child\_ettle\_id or parent\_id MUST\\n    be updated to use the new field names and link model.\\n\\n## 6. Leaf EP definition \(updated\)\\n\\n  A leaf EP is an EP that has no child EPs — i.e., no other EP has parent\_ep\_id\\n  pointing to it. This replaces the previous definition \(leaf EP = EP with\\n  child\_ettle\_id = null\). All code that detects leaf status MUST use the new definition.\\n\\n## 7. MCP and CLI layer\\n\\n  - MCP \(ettlex.apply\) MUST accept all new command fields defined in section 4.\\n  - MCP MUST NOT implement any validation logic beyond schema validation \(types,\\n    required fields\). All semantic validation \(IC-1 through IC-6, tombstone guards\)\\n    lives in the action layer.\\n  - CLI MUST provide thin wrappers for all six commands \(EttleCreate, EttleUpdate,\\n    EttleTombstone, EpCreate, EpUpdate, EpTombstone\). No business logic in CLI.\\n  - MCP tool ettle.get response MUST include parent\_ettle\_id \(not parent\_id\).\\n  - MCP tool ep.get response MUST include containing\_ettle \(not ettle\_id\) and\\n    parent\_ep\_id \(not child\_ettle\_id\).\\n\\n## 8. Expected Failure Registry \(pre-authorised; see HOW for #\[ignore\] protocol\)\\n\\nThe following test files contain scenarios that WILL fail as a direct consequence of\\nthis migration. They are pre-authorised failures. seed parser writes ettle\_id and child\_ettle\_id columns.\\n  EFR-12: ettlex-store/tests/migrations\_test.rs\\n          Reason: asserts on schema shape after migrations 009/010 which are ettlex-engine/tests/ep\_update\_engine\_tests.rs\\n          Reason: references ettle\_id and child\_ettle\_id in engine-level EP tests.","why":"The current Ettle/EP schema uses field names and link structures that are semantically incorrect and operationally obtuse:\\n\\n  - \`eps.ettle\_id\` is an opaque foreign key with no semantic clarity about the direction of membership.\\n  - \`eps.child\_ettle\_id\` encodes a refinement link from an EP to a child Ettle, but the correct model is\\n    EP-to-EP refinement across Ettle boundaries, not EP-to-Ettle.\\n  - \`ettles.parent\_id\` duplicates information derivable from the EP tree and conflates two independent\\n    link trees: the Ettle abstraction-level hierarchy and the EP refinement trace.\\n  - \`ettles.parent\_ep\_id\` \(migration 009\) partially corrected this but conflated the two trees further.\\n  - The MCP and CLI command vocabulary \(\`EttleCreate\`, \`EpCreate\`, \`EpUpdate\`\) do not expose the structural\\n    link fields at all, forcing seed import as the only path to establish refinement relationships.\\n    This is the root cause of the tree corruption discovered in prior sessions.\\n  - \`eps.content\_digest\` and \`eps.content\_inline\` are a dual-storage pattern that is unnecessary;\\n    WHY/WHAT/HOW are already surfaced as JSON in the \`content\` field at the MCP layer.\\n\\nThis Ettle corrects the structural model and exposes full CRUD for both Ettles and EPs — including all\\nlink fields — through the command vocabulary \(Apply\) and query surfaces, so the MCP and CLI become the\\ncanonical authoring path and seed import is no longer required for structural operations.\\n\\nNon-goals \(explicitly out of scope for this Ettle\):\\n  - EPT computation changes \(ept.compute, ept\_digest, snapshot commit traversal\).\\n  - Snapshot manifest changes.\\n  - Constraint, decision, profile, approval, or policy entity changes.\\n  - DAG support for EP or Ettle parent links \(deferred; strict trees only\).\\n  - CLI UX beyond thin command wiring.\\n  - Seed importer changes or retirement.\\n  - Any existing test modification beyond #\[ignore\]-tagging of pre-authorised failures\\n    \(see WHAT section: Expected Failure Registry\)."} | 0 | 1773001042 | 1773008222 | null | ettle:019ccf15-e2b1-7e33-9794-bf2cf0704178 | Schema Migration 012 — Ettle/EP Structural Model I call ettle.get\(E\)\\n  Then response contains id, title, why=\\"W\\", what=\\"X\\", how=\\"H\\"\\n  And reasoning\_link\_id is null, tombstoned\_at is null\\n\\nScenario: EttleGet returns tombstoned record with tombstoned\_at set\\n  Given Ettle E is tombstoned\\n  When I call ettle.get\(E\)\\n  Then response contains tombstoned\_at as non-null timestamp\\n\\nScenario: EttleGet returns NotFound for unknown id\\n  When I call ettle.get\(\\"ettle:unknown\\"\)\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\\n### Feature: EttleList\\n\\nScenario: EttleList returns active Ettles in deterministic order\\n  Given Ettles A and B exist \(A created before B\)\\n  When I call ettle.list\(\)\\n  Then response items are \[A, B\] in created\_at ASC order\\n  And tombstoned Ettles are excluded\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with include\_tombstoned returns all\\n  Given Ettle A is active, Ettle B is tombstoned\\n  When I call ettle.list\(include\_tombstoned: true\)\\n  Then response contains both A and B\\n\\nScenario: EttleList pagination is deterministic\\n  Given 10 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 5\)\\n  Then 5 items are returned and a cursor is present\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 5, cursor: &lt;cursor&gt;\)\\n  Then the next 5 items are returned with no cursor\\n  And no item appears in both pages\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with invalid cursor returns error\\n  When I call ettle.list\(cursor: \\"not-valid-base64!!\\"\)\\n  Then error kind InvalidInput is returned\\n\\n### Feature: EttleUpdate\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate changes title\\n  Given Ettle E with title \\"Old\\"\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, title: \\"New\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).title = \\"New\\"\\n  And state\_version increments by 1\\n  And provenance event ettle\_updated is recorded\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate changes WHY/WHAT/HOW\\n  Given Ettle E\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, why: \\"W2\\", what: \\"X2\\", how: \\"H2\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\) returns why=\\"W2\\", what=\\"X2\\", how=\\"H2\\"\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate sets reasoning\_link\_id\\n  Given Ettle E and Ettle P both exist\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: P, reasoning\_link\_type: \\"option\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_id = P\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_type = \\"option\\"\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate clears reasoning\_link\_id\\n  Given Ettle E has reasoning\_link\_id = P\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: null }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_id is null\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_type is null\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects self-referential reasoning\_link\_id\\n  Given Ettle E\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_type: \\"refinement\\" }\\n  Then error kind SelfReferentialLink is returned\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_id is unchanged\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects reasoning\_link\_id without reasoning\_link\_type\\n  Given Ettle E and Ettle P\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: P }\\n  Then error kind MissingLinkType is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects update to non-existent Ettle\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: \\"ettle:missing\\", title: \\"X\\" }\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects update to tombstoned Ettle\\n  Given Ettle E is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, title: \\"X\\" }\\n  Then error kind AlreadyTombstoned is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate with no fields supplied is rejected\\n  Given Ettle E\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E } with no optional fields\\n  Then error kind InvalidInput is returned\\n\\n### Feature: EttleTombstone\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone marks Ettle inactive; row retained\\n  Given Ettle E with no active dependants\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: E }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).tombstoned\_at is non-null\\n  And the row still exists in the database\\n  And state\_version increments by 1\\n  And provenance event ettle\_tombstoned is recorded\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone rejects Ettle with active dependants\\n  Given Ettle P, Ettle C with reasoning\_link\_id = P\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: P }\\n  Then error kind HasActiveDependants is returned\\n  And ettle.get\(P\).tombstoned\_at is null\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone allows tombstone when dependant is itself tombstoned\\n  Given Ettle P, Ettle C with reasoning\_link\_id = P and C is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: P }\\n  Then the command succeeds\\n  And ettle.get\(P\).tombstoned\_at is non-null\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone rejects already-tombstoned Ettle\\n  Given Ettle E is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: E }\\n  Then error kind AlreadyTombstoned is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone rejects non-existent Ettle\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: \\"ettle:missing\\" }\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\\n### Feature: OCC \(Optimistic Concurrency\)\\n\\nScenario: Command with correct expected\_state\_version succeeds\\n  Given state\_version is V\\n  When I apply any write command with expected\_state\_version = V\\n  Then the command succeeds and new\_state\_version = V + 1\\n\\nScenario: Command with wrong expected\_state\_version fails\\n  Given state\_version is V\\n  When I apply any write command with expected\_state\_version = V - 1\\n  Then error kind HeadMismatch is returned\\n  And state\_version remains V\\n\\n### Feature: Provenance\\n\\nScenario: Each successful mutation appends exactly one provenance event\\n  When I apply any of EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone successfully\\n  Then exactly one provenance\_event row is appended\\n  And the event kind matches the command\\n\\nScenario: Failed commands append no provenance events\\n  When I apply a command that returns any typed error\\n  Then no provenance\_event row is appended\\n\\n### Feature: Migration\\n\\nScenario: Migration applies cleanly on top of existing migrations\\n  Given a database with all prior migrations applied\\n  When the new migration is applied\\n  Then no error occurs\\n  And the ettles table has columns why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, tombstoned\_at\\n  And existing rows have why='', what='', how='', reasoning\_link\_id=NULL, reasoning\_link\_type=NULL, tombstoned\_at=NULL\\n\\n## MCP Response Shapes\\n\\n### ettle.get response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{\\n  \\"id\\": \\"ettle:...\\",\\n  \\"title\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"why\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"what\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"how\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"reasoning\_link\_id\\": null,\\n  \\"reasoning\_link\_type\\": null,\\n  \\"created\_at\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"updated\_at\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"tombstoned\_at\\": null\\n}\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettle.list response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{\\n  \\"items\\": \[\\n    { \\"id\\": \\"ettle:...\\", \\"title\\": \\"...\\", \\"tombstoned\_at\\": null }\\n  \],\\n  \\"cursor\\": \\"&lt;opaque base64 or absent&gt;\\"\\n}\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettlex.apply EttleCreate response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{ \\"new\_state\_version\\": 1, \\"result\\": { \\"tag\\": \\"EttleCreate\\", \\"ettle\_id\\": \\"ettle:...\\" } }\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettlex.apply EttleUpdate response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{ \\"new\_state\_version\\": 2, \\"result\\": { \\"tag\\": \\"EttleUpdate\\" } }\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettlex.apply EttleTombstone response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{ \\"new\_state\_version\\": 3, \\"result\\": { \\"tag\\": \\"EttleTombstone\\" } }\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n## Expected Failure Registry \(pre-authorised\)\\n\\nThe following test files will fail as a direct consequence of this slice and MUST be #\[ignore\]-tagged or excluded via the Makefile SLICE\_TEST\_FILTER. The code generator MUST NOT modify their test logic.\\n\\nEFR-01: All tests in ettlex-engine/tests/ that reference old Ettle field names \(parent\_id, ettle\_id on EPs used as Ettle ID, deleted boolean\) or old command shapes without WHY/WHAT/HOW.\\nEFR-02: All tests in ettlex-store/tests/ that assert on the old ettles table schema \(absence of why/what/how columns, presence of deleted column without tombstoned\_at\).\\nEFR-03: MCP integration tests in ettlex-mcp/tests/ that assert ettle.get or ettle.list response shapes without the new fields.\\n\\nThe code generator MUST enumerate each specific test function in the Pre-Authorised Failure Registry section of the completion report.","what":"## Scope\\n\\nThis slice implements full Ettle CRUD across Store, Engine/Action, and MCP layers:\\n- EttleCreate\\n- EttleGet\\n- EttleList \(paginated, deterministic\)\\n- EttleUpdate \(title, why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type\)\\n- EttleTombstone \(with dependant check\)\\n\\nHard delete is out of scope \(deferred pending Profile system\).\\nEP CRUD is out of scope.\\nRelation CRUD is out of scope \(Reasoning Link fields are stored on the Ettle record but the full Relation model is a future slice\).\\n\\n## New Ettle Record Shape\\n\\nThe Ettle record at the store layer carries:\\n- id \(TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ettle: prefix, ULIDv7\)\\n- title \(TEXT NOT NULL\)\\n- why \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- what \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- how \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- reasoning\_link\_id \(TEXT NULL, FK → ettles.id\)\\n- reasoning\_link\_type \(TEXT NULL, e.g. 'refinement' \| 'option'\)\\n- created\_at \(TEXT NOT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n- updated\_at \(TEXT NOT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n- tombstoned\_at \(TEXT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n\\n## Migration\\n\\nA new migration adds WHY/WHAT/HOW columns and reasoning\_link\_id/reasoning\_link\_type to the existing ettles table. The tombstoned\_at column replaces the deleted boolean. All existing rows receive empty strings for WHY/WHAT/HOW and NULL for tombstoned\_at and reasoning link fields.\\n\\nMigration MUST be additive. Existing rows MUST survive.\\n\\n## Command Vocabulary \(Action Layer\)\\n\\n### EttleCreate\\nInput: title \(required, non-empty\), why \(optional, default ''\), what \(optional, default ''\), how \(optional, default ''\), reasoning\_link\_id \(optional, nullable\), reasoning\_link\_type \(optional, nullable, required if reasoning\_link\_id is set\)\\nOutput: { ettle\_id }\\nInvariants:\\n- title must be non-empty\\n- ettle\_id is auto-generated \(ULIDv7 prefixed ettle:\)\\n- Caller must not supply ettle\_id\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is supplied, referenced Ettle must exist and must not be tombstoned\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is supplied, reasoning\_link\_type must also be supplied\\n- reasoning\_link\_type must be a non-empty string when supplied\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_created appended\\n\\n### EttleGet\\nInput: ettle\_id\\nOutput: { id, title, why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, created\_at, updated\_at, tombstoned\_at }\\nInvariants:\\n- Returns NotFound if ettle\_id does not exist\\n- Returns the record including tombstoned records \(caller sees tombstoned\_at\)\\n- No state\_version increment \(read-only\)\\n\\n### EttleList\\nInput: limit \(optional, default 100, max 1000\), cursor \(optional, opaque base64\)\\nOutput: { items: \[{ id, title, tombstoned\_at }\], cursor? }\\nInvariants:\\n- Ordering: \(created\_at ASC, id ASC\) — deterministic\\n- Excludes tombstoned records by default\\n- include\_tombstoned \(optional bool, default false\) includes tombstoned records\\n- Cursor is opaque base64-encoded \(created\_at, id\) pair\\n- No state\_version increment \(read-only\)\\n\\n### EttleUpdate\\nInput: ettle\_id \(required\), title \(optional\), why \(optional\), what \(optional\), how \(optional\), reasoning\_link\_id \(optional, null clears the link\), reasoning\_link\_type \(optional, null clears the type\)\\nOutput: {}\\nInvariants:\\n- At least one field must be supplied\\n- ettle\_id must exist\\n- ettle\_id must not be tombstoned\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is set to a non-null value, referenced Ettle must exist and not be tombstoned\\n- An Ettle must not be set as its own reasoning\_link\_id \(self-referential link rejected with SelfReferentialLink\)\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is cleared \(null\), reasoning\_link\_type is also cleared regardless of whether reasoning\_link\_type is supplied\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is set, reasoning\_link\_type must be supplied and non-empty\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_updated appended\\n\\n### EttleTombstone\\nInput: ettle\_id \(required\)\\nOutput: {}\\nInvariants:\\n- ettle\_id must exist\\n- ettle\_id must not already be tombstoned \(AlreadyTombstoned\)\\n- Ettle must have no active \(non-tombstoned\) dependants: no other Ettle has this as reasoning\_link\_id\\n- Row is retained; tombstoned\_at is set to current UTC timestamp\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_tombstoned appended\\n\\n## Error Kinds Used\\n\\nAll from ExErrorKind \(canonical error taxonomy\):\\n- InvalidInput — empty title, missing required fields\\n- InvalidTitle — title is whitespace-only\\n- NotFound — ettle\_id does not exist\\n- AlreadyTombstoned — EttleTombstone on an already-tombstoned Ettle\\n- SelfReferentialLink — reasoning\_link\_id set to own ettle\_id\\n- HasActiveDependants — EttleTombstone blocked by active child Ettles\\n- MissingLinkType — reasoning\_link\_id supplied without reasoning\_link\_type\\n\\nNote: SelfReferentialLink and AlreadyTombstoned and MissingLinkType are new error kinds to be added to ExErrorKind.\\n\\n## Layer Responsibilities\\n\\n### Store \(ettlex-store\)\\n- Migration adding new columns\\n- EttleRow struct updated\\n- Store functions: insert\_ettle, get\_ettle, list\_ettles, update\_ettle, tombstone\_ettle\\n- All functions return Result&lt;\_, ExError&gt;\\n- No business logic; structural integrity only \(FK existence, uniqueness\)\\n\\n### Engine/Action \(ettlex-engine\)\\n- EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone command handlers\\n- EttleGet, EttleList query handlers\\n- Invariant enforcement \(all IC rules above\)\\n- state\_version increment via mcp\_command\_log\\n- Provenance event append\\n- Dependant check for tombstone: query store for Ettles with reasoning\_link\_id = this ettle\_id\\n\\n### MCP \(ettlex-mcp\)\\n- ettlex.apply accepts EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone\\n- ettle.get and ettle.list tools updated to return new field set\\n- Schema validation only at MCP layer; all semantic validation in engine\\n- Response shapes use new field names throughout\\n\\n## Out of Scope\\n\\n- Hard delete \(deferred pending Profile system\)\\n- Cycle detection in reasoning\_link\_id chains \(deferred to Reasoning Path slice\)\\n- EP CRUD \(legacy construct, phased out\)\\n- Relation CRUD \(future slice\)\\n- Snapshot commit changes\\n- Decision, Constraint, Group CRUD\\n- CLI wiring \(future slice\)","why":"The existing Ettle CRUD implementation was written against the original schema and domain model. It conflates EP structure with Ettle identity, uses field names that no longer exist \(parent\_id, ettle\_id on EPs\), and lacks WHY/WHAT/HOW fields on the Ettle record itself. The new conceptual model \(v0.8\) places WHY, WHAT, and HOW directly on the Ettle record as the primary reasoning content, introduces a Reasoning Link \(reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type\) for parent traversal, and uses tombstoned\_at consistently across all governed records.\\n\\nThe vertical slice approach requires a full replacement of the Ettle CRUD path — Store, Engine/Action, and MCP — as a coherent unit. All layers must reflect the new model simultaneously. Existing implementations of ettle\_get, ettle\_list, EttleCreate, and EttleUpdate are replaced. Pre-authorised failures for all tests that reference the old schema are registered and tagged.\\n\\nHard delete is deferred: the Profile system required to govern it is not part of this slice. Tombstone is the only deletion path in this slice.\\n\\nEP CRUD is explicitly out of scope for this slice. EPs are a legacy construct being phased out; the new model stores reasoning content directly on the Ettle record."} | 0 | 1773526415 | 1773526415 | null | ettle:019cee68-3061-7900-80a5-fa8257becb57 | Slice 01 — Ettle CRUD \(Store → Engine/Action → MCP\) | null | 0 | 2026-03-14T22:12:11Z | 2026-03-14T22:12:11Z | {"data":{}} | null |  |  |  | null | null | 2026-03-22T19:40:58.909321+00:00 |
