EttleGet returns NotFound for unknown id\\n  When I call ettle.get\(\\"ettle:unknown\\"\)\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleGet is deterministic across repeated calls\\n  Given Ettle E exists\\n  When I call ettle.get\(E\) twice in succession without modifying state\\n  Then both responses are byte-identical JSON\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleList — happy path and ordering\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleList returns active Ettles in deterministic order\\n  Given Ettles A and B exist \(A created before B\)\\n  When I call ettle.list\(\)\\n  Then response items are \[A, B\] in created\_at ASC order\\n  And tombstoned Ettles are excluded\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with include\_tombstoned returns all\\n  Given Ettle A is active, Ettle B is tombstoned\\n  When I call ettle.list\(include\_tombstoned: true\)\\n  Then response contains both A and B\\n\\nScenario: EttleList is deterministic across repeated calls\\n  Given 5 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(\) twice without modifying state\\n  Then both responses are byte-identical JSON\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleList — pagination\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleList pagination is deterministic\\n  Given 10 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 5\)\\n  Then 5 items are returned and a cursor is present\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 5, cursor: &lt;cursor&gt;\)\\n  Then the next 5 items are returned with no cursor\\n  And no item appears in both pages\\n\\nScenario: EttleList last page returns no cursor\\n  Given 3 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 5\)\\n  Then 3 items are returned and no cursor is present\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with limit=1 returns single item\\n  Given at least 2 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 1\)\\n  Then exactly 1 item is returned and a cursor is present\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with limit=1000 succeeds\\n  Given any number of Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 1000\)\\n  Then the command succeeds and returns at most 1000 items\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleList — boundary and negative cases\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleList with limit=0 is rejected\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 0\)\\n  Then error kind InvalidInput is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with limit exceeding maximum is rejected\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 1001\)\\n  Then error kind InvalidInput is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleList with invalid cursor returns error\\n  When I call ettle.list\(cursor: \\"not-valid-base64!!\\"\)\\n  Then error kind InvalidInput is returned\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleUpdate — happy path\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleUpdate changes title\\n  Given Ettle E with title \\"Old\\"\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, title: \\"New\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).title = \\"New\\"\\n  And state\_version increments by 1\\n  And provenance event ettle\_updated is recorded\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate changes WHY/WHAT/HOW\\n  Given Ettle E\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, why: \\"W2\\", what: \\"X2\\", how: \\"H2\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\) returns why=\\"W2\\", what=\\"X2\\", how=\\"H2\\"\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate sets reasoning\_link\_id\\n  Given Ettle E and Ettle P both exist\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: P, reasoning\_link\_type: \\"option\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_id = P\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_type = \\"option\\"\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate clears reasoning\_link\_id\\n  Given Ettle E has reasoning\_link\_id = P\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: null }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_id is null\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_type is null\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate preserves unspecified fields\\n  Given Ettle E with title=\\"T\\", why=\\"W\\", what=\\"X\\", how=\\"H\\"\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, title: \\"T2\\" }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).why = \\"W\\"\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).what = \\"X\\"\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).how = \\"H\\"\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleUpdate — negative and error paths\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects self-referential reasoning\_link\_id\\n  Given Ettle E\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_type: \\"refinement\\" }\\n  Then error kind SelfReferentialLink is returned\\n  And ettle.get\(E\).reasoning\_link\_id is unchanged\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects reasoning\_link\_id without reasoning\_link\_type\\n  Given Ettle E and Ettle P\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, reasoning\_link\_id: P }\\n  Then error kind MissingLinkType is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects update to non-existent Ettle\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: \\"ettle:missing\\", title: \\"X\\" }\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate rejects update to tombstoned Ettle\\n  Given Ettle E is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, title: \\"X\\" }\\n  Then error kind AlreadyTombstoned is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleUpdate with no fields supplied is rejected\\n  Given Ettle E\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E } with no optional fields\\n  Then error kind InvalidInput is returned\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleTombstone — happy path and state transitions\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleTombstone marks Ettle inactive; row retained\\n  Given Ettle E with no active dependants\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: E }\\n  Then ettle.get\(E\).tombstoned\_at is non-null\\n  And the row still exists in the database\\n  And state\_version increments by 1\\n  And provenance event ettle\_tombstoned is recorded\\n\\nScenario: Tombstoned Ettle cannot be updated\\n  Given Ettle E is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleUpdate { ettle\_id: E, title: \\"X\\" }\\n  Then error kind AlreadyTombstoned is returned\\n\\nScenario: Tombstoned Ettle cannot be tombstoned again\\n  Given Ettle E is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: E }\\n  Then error kind AlreadyTombstoned is returned\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone allows tombstone when dependant is itself tombstoned\\n  Given Ettle P, Ettle C with reasoning\_link\_id = P and C is tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: P }\\n  Then the command succeeds\\n  And ettle.get\(P\).tombstoned\_at is non-null\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: EttleTombstone — negative cases\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleTombstone rejects Ettle with active dependants\\n  Given Ettle P, Ettle C with reasoning\_link\_id = P and C is not tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: P }\\n  Then error kind HasActiveDependants is returned\\n  And ettle.get\(P\).tombstoned\_at is null\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone rejects non-existent Ettle\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: \\"ettle:missing\\" }\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Hard delete prohibition\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Hard delete is not exposed via MCP in this slice\\n  When I attempt to invoke any hard delete operation via ettlex.apply\\n  Then the command is not recognised \(error kind InvalidInput or command not found\)\\n  And no row is deleted from the database\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: OCC \(Optimistic Concurrency\)\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Command with correct expected\_state\_version succeeds\\n  Given state\_version is V\\n  When I apply any write command with expected\_state\_version = V\\n  Then the command succeeds and new\_state\_version = V + 1\\n\\nScenario: Command with wrong expected\_state\_version fails\\n  Given state\_version is V\\n  When I apply any write command with expected\_state\_version = V - 1\\n  Then error kind HeadMismatch is returned\\n  And state\_version remains V\\n  And no provenance event is appended\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Provenance / observability\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Each successful mutation appends exactly one provenance event\\n  When I apply any of EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone successfully\\n  Then exactly one provenance\_event row is appended\\n  And the event kind matches the command \(ettle\_created, ettle\_updated, ettle\_tombstoned\)\\n\\nScenario: Failed commands append no provenance events\\n  When I apply a command that returns any typed error\\n  Then no provenance\_event row is appended\\n  And the total provenance\_event count is unchanged\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Deterministic byte-level output\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleGet output is byte-identical across repeated calls\\n  Given Ettle E exists with all fields populated\\n  When I call ettle.get\(E\) twice without modifying state\\n  Then the JSON responses are byte-identical\\n  And field ordering in the JSON is stable\\n\\nScenario: EttleList output is byte-identical across repeated calls\\n  Given 5 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(\) twice without modifying state\\n  Then the JSON responses are byte-identical\\n  And item ordering is stable\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Resource limits\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleCreate with large WHY/WHAT/HOW fields succeeds\\n  When I apply EttleCreate { title: \\"T\\", why: &lt;100KB string&gt;, what: &lt;100KB string&gt;, how: &lt;100KB string&gt; }\\n  Then the command succeeds within the configured time budget\\n  And ettle.get returns all three fields fully and correctly\\n\\nScenario: EttleList at maximum limit succeeds within time budget\\n  Given 1000 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(limit: 1000\)\\n  Then 1000 items are returned and the call completes within the configured time budget\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Migration\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Migration applies cleanly on top of existing migrations\\n  Given a database with all prior migrations applied\\n  When the new migration is applied\\n  Then no error occurs\\n  And the ettles table has columns why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, tombstoned\_at\\n  And the deleted column is absent \(replaced by tombstoned\_at\)\\n  And existing rows have why='', what='', how='', reasoning\_link\_id=NULL, reasoning\_link\_type=NULL, tombstoned\_at=NULL\\n\\nScenario: Pre-existing Ettle rows survive migration with values preserved\\n  Given Ettle rows exist before the migration with id and title populated\\n  When the migration is applied\\n  Then all pre-existing rows are present\\n  And their id and title values are unchanged\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n## MCP Response Shapes\\n\\n### ettle.get response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{\\n  \\"id\\": \\"ettle:...\\",\\n  \\"title\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"why\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"what\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"how\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"reasoning\_link\_id\\": null,\\n  \\"reasoning\_link\_type\\": null,\\n  \\"created\_at\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"updated\_at\\": \\"...\\",\\n  \\"tombstoned\_at\\": null\\n}\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettle.list response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{\\n  \\"items\\": \[\\n    { \\"id\\": \\"ettle:...\\", \\"title\\": \\"...\\", \\"tombstoned\_at\\": null }\\n  \],\\n  \\"cursor\\": \\"&lt;opaque base64 or absent&gt;\\"\\n}\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettlex.apply EttleCreate response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{ \\"new\_state\_version\\": 1, \\"result\\": { \\"tag\\": \\"EttleCreate\\", \\"ettle\_id\\": \\"ettle:...\\" } }\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettlex.apply EttleUpdate response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{ \\"new\_state\_version\\": 2, \\"result\\": { \\"tag\\": \\"EttleUpdate\\" } }\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### ettlex.apply EttleTombstone response\\n\`\`\`json\\n{ \\"new\_state\_version\\": 3, \\"result\\": { \\"tag\\": \\"EttleTombstone\\" } }\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n## Expected Failure Registry \(pre-authorised\)\\n\\nThe following test files will fail as a direct consequence of this slice and MUST be excluded via the Makefile SLICE\_TEST\_FILTER. The code generator MUST NOT modify their test logic.\\n\\nEFR-01: All tests in ettlex-engine/tests/ that reference old Ettle field names \(parent\_id, ettle\_id on EPs used as Ettle ID, deleted boolean\) or old command shapes without WHY/WHAT/HOW.\\nEFR-02: All tests in ettlex-store/tests/ that assert on the old ettles table schema \(absence of why/what/how columns, presence of deleted column without tombstoned\_at\).\\nEFR-03: MCP integration tests in ettlex-mcp/tests/ that assert ettle.get or ettle.list response shapes without the new fields.\\n\\nThe code generator MUST enumerate each specific test function in the Pre-Authorised Failure Registry section of the completion report.","what":"## Scope\\n\\nThis slice implements full Ettle CRUD across Store, Engine/Action, and MCP layers:\\n- EttleCreate\\n- EttleGet\\n- EttleList \(paginated, deterministic\)\\n- EttleUpdate \(title, why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type\)\\n- EttleTombstone \(with dependant check\)\\n\\nHard delete is out of scope \(deferred pending Profile system\).\\nEP CRUD is out of scope.\\nRelation CRUD is out of scope \(Reasoning Link fields are stored on the Ettle record but the full Relation model is a future slice\).\\n\\n## New Ettle Record Shape\\n\\nThe Ettle record at the store layer carries:\\n- id \(TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ettle: prefix, ULIDv7\)\\n- title \(TEXT NOT NULL\)\\n- why \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- what \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- how \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- reasoning\_link\_id \(TEXT NULL, FK → ettles.id\)\\n- reasoning\_link\_type \(TEXT NULL, e.g. 'refinement' \| 'option'\)\\n- created\_at \(TEXT NOT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n- updated\_at \(TEXT NOT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n- tombstoned\_at \(TEXT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n\\n## Migration\\n\\nA new migration adds WHY/WHAT/HOW columns and reasoning\_link\_id/reasoning\_link\_type to the existing ettles table. The tombstoned\_at column replaces the deleted boolean. All existing rows receive empty strings for WHY/WHAT/HOW and NULL for tombstoned\_at and reasoning link fields.\\n\\nMigration MUST be additive. Existing rows MUST survive.\\n\\n## Command Vocabulary \(Action Layer\)\\n\\n### EttleCreate\\nInput: title \(required, non-empty\), why \(optional, default ''\), what \(optional, default ''\), how \(optional, default ''\), reasoning\_link\_id \(optional, nullable\), reasoning\_link\_type \(optional, nullable, required if reasoning\_link\_id is set\)\\nOutput: { ettle\_id }\\nInvariants:\\n- title must be non-empty after trimming whitespace\\n- ettle\_id is auto-generated \(ULIDv7 prefixed ettle:\)\\n- Caller must not supply ettle\_id\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is supplied, referenced Ettle must exist and must not be tombstoned\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is supplied, reasoning\_link\_type must also be supplied\\n- reasoning\_link\_type must be a non-empty string when supplied\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_created appended\\n\\n### EttleGet\\nInput: ettle\_id\\nOutput: { id, title, why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, created\_at, updated\_at, tombstoned\_at }\\nInvariants:\\n- Returns NotFound if ettle\_id does not exist\\n- Returns the record including tombstoned records \(caller sees tombstoned\_at\)\\n- No state\_version increment \(read-only\)\\n- Repeated calls with the same ettle\_id return byte-identical JSON output for identical canonical state\\n\\n### EttleList\\nInput: limit \(optional, default 100, min 1, max 1000\), cursor \(optional, opaque base64\), include\_tombstoned \(optional bool, default false\)\\nOutput: { items: \[{ id, title, tombstoned\_at }\], cursor? }\\nInvariants:\\n- Ordering: \(created\_at ASC, id ASC\) — deterministic\\n- Excludes tombstoned records by default\\n- include\_tombstoned=true includes tombstoned records\\n- Cursor is opaque base64-encoded \(created\_at, id\) pair\\n- No state\_version increment \(read-only\)\\n- Repeated calls with identical parameters and identical canonical state return byte-identical JSON output\\n- limit=1 is valid and returns at most one item\\n- limit=1000 is the maximum; limit=1001 is rejected with InvalidInput\\n- limit=0 is rejected with InvalidInput\\n- Negative limit is rejected with InvalidInput\\n\\n### EttleUpdate\\nInput: ettle\_id \(required\), title \(optional\), why \(optional\), what \(optional\), how \(optional\), reasoning\_link\_id \(optional, null clears the link\), reasoning\_link\_type \(optional, null clears the type\)\\nOutput: {}\\nInvariants:\\n- At least one field must be supplied\\n- ettle\_id must exist\\n- ettle\_id must not be tombstoned\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is set to a non-null value, referenced Ettle must exist and not be tombstoned\\n- An Ettle must not be set as its own reasoning\_link\_id \(self-referential link rejected with SelfReferentialLink\)\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is cleared \(null\), reasoning\_link\_type is also cleared regardless of whether reasoning\_link\_type is supplied\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is set, reasoning\_link\_type must be supplied and non-empty\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_updated appended\\n\\n### EttleTombstone\\nInput: ettle\_id \(required\)\\nOutput: {}\\nInvariants:\\n- ettle\_id must exist\\n- ettle\_id must not already be tombstoned \(AlreadyTombstoned\)\\n- Ettle must have no active \(non-tombstoned\) dependants: no other Ettle has this as reasoning\_link\_id\\n- Row is retained; tombstoned\_at is set to current UTC timestamp\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_tombstoned appended\\n\\n## Error Kinds Used\\n\\nAll from ExErrorKind \(canonical error taxonomy\):\\n- InvalidInput — missing required fields, invalid limit values, caller-supplied ettle\_id, no fields in update\\n- InvalidTitle — title is empty or whitespace-only\\n- NotFound — ettle\_id does not exist\\n- AlreadyTombstoned — EttleTombstone on an already-tombstoned Ettle; or EttleCreate/EttleUpdate referencing a tombstoned Ettle as reasoning\_link\_id\\n- SelfReferentialLink — reasoning\_link\_id set to own ettle\_id\\n- HasActiveDependants — EttleTombstone blocked by active child Ettles\\n- MissingLinkType — reasoning\_link\_id supplied without reasoning\_link\_type\\n- HeadMismatch — expected\_state\_version does not match current state\_version\\n\\nNote: SelfReferentialLink, AlreadyTombstoned, and MissingLinkType are new error kinds to be added to ExErrorKind.\\n\\n## Concurrency Model\\n\\nSQLite with rusqlite \(bundled\) serialises all write operations at the database level. True simultaneous concurrent writes are not possible. The OCC \(optimistic concurrency control\) mechanism via expected\_state\_version provides an additional application-level guard for clients that wish to assert they are operating on a known version of state. No additional concurrency primitives are required in this slice.\\n\\n## Layer Responsibilities\\n\\n### Store \(ettlex-store\)\\n- Migration adding new columns\\n- EttleRow struct updated\\n- Store functions: insert\_ettle, get\_ettle, list\_ettles, update\_ettle, tombstone\_ettle\\n- All functions return Result&lt;\_, ExError&gt;\\n- No business logic; structural integrity only \(FK existence, uniqueness\)\\n\\n### Engine/Action \(ettlex-engine\)\\n- EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone command handlers\\n- EttleGet, EttleList query handlers\\n- Invariant enforcement \(all IC rules above\)\\n- state\_version increment via mcp\_command\_log\\n- Provenance event append\\n- Dependant check for tombstone: query store for Ettles with reasoning\_link\_id = this ettle\_id where tombstoned\_at IS NULL\\n\\n### MCP \(ettlex-mcp\)\\n- ettlex.apply accepts EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone\\n- ettle.get and ettle.list tools updated to return new field set\\n- Schema validation only at MCP layer; all semantic validation in engine\\n- Response shapes use new field names throughout\\n- Hard delete is NOT exposed via MCP in this slice; any attempt to invoke a hard delete operation MUST return an error\\n\\n## Out of Scope\\n\\n- Hard delete \(deferred pending Profile system\)\\n- Cycle detection in reasoning\_link\_id chains \(deferred to Reasoning Path slice\)\\n- EP CRUD \(legacy construct, phased out\)\\n- Relation CRUD \(future slice\)\\n- Snapshot commit changes\\n- Decision, Constraint, Group CRUD\\n- CLI wiring \(future slice\)\\n- Authentication and authorisation \(future slice\)","why":"The existing Ettle CRUD implementation was written against the original schema and domain model. It conflates EP structure with Ettle identity, uses field names that no longer exist \(parent\_id, ettle\_id on EPs\), and lacks WHY/WHAT/HOW fields on the Ettle record itself. The new conceptual model \(v0.8\) places WHY, WHAT, and HOW directly on the Ettle record as the primary reasoning content, introduces a Reasoning Link \(reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type\) for parent traversal, and uses tombstoned\_at consistently across all governed records.\\n\\nThe vertical slice approach requires a full replacement of the Ettle CRUD path — Store, Engine/Action, and MCP — as a coherent unit. All layers must reflect the new model simultaneously. Existing implementations of ettle\_get, ettle\_list, EttleCreate, and EttleUpdate are replaced. Pre-authorised failures for all tests that reference the old schema are registered and tagged.\\n\\nHard delete is deferred: the Profile system required to govern it is not part of this slice. Tombstone is the only deletion path in this slice.\\n\\nEP CRUD is explicitly out of scope for this slice. EPs are a legacy construct being phased out; the new model stores reasoning content directly on the Ettle record."} | 0 | 1773528612 | 1773528612 | null | ettle:019cee89-4b89-7bc2-9855-0ca85605df5a | Slice 01 — Ettle CRUD \(Store → Engine/Action → MCP\) v2 | null | 0 | 2026-03-14T22:48:21Z | 2026-03-14T22:48:21Z | {"data":{}} | null |  |  |  | null | null | 2026-03-22T19:41:02.988764+00:00 |

Some\(\\"ettle:1\\"\)\\n  And ex.message\(\) == \\"not found\\"\\n  And ex.code\(\) == \\"ERR\_NOT\_FOUND\\"\\n\\nScenario: assert\_err\_kind! macro passes on correct kind\\n  Given a message\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: New ExErrorKind variants\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: AlreadyTombstoned has correct stable code\\n  When I call ExErrorKind::AlreadyTombstoned.code\(\)\\n  Then the result is \\"ERR\_ALREADY\_TOMBSTONED\\"\\n\\nScenario: SelfReferentialLink has correct stable code\\n  When I call ExErrorKind::SelfReferentialLink.code\(\)\\n  Then the result is \\"ERR\_SELF\_REFERENTIAL\_LINK\\"\\n\\nScenario: HasActiveDependants has correct stable code\\n  When I call ExErrorKind::HasActiveDependants.code\(\)\\n  Then the result is \\"ERR\_HAS\_ACTIVE\_DEPENDANTS\\"\\n\\nScenario: MissingLinkType has correct stable code\\n  When I call ExErrorKind::MissingLinkType.code\(\)\\n  Then the result is The code generator MUST migrate these tests to use \`ExError\` as part of this slice, since the retirement of \`EttleXError\` is within the slice boundary.\\n\\nNote: Unlike feature slices, this infrastructure slice is permitted to update test files that reference \`EttleXError\` because the retirement of \`EttleXError\` is the explicit intent of the slice. The coexistence rule applies to code \*outside\* the slice boundary; \`EttleXError\` references anywhere in the workspace are within scope for this slice.","what":"## Scope\\n\\nThis slice performs the following structural changes:\\n\\n1. Extract \`logging\_facility\` from \`ettlex-core\` into a new standalone \`ettlex-logging\` crate\\n2. Extract \`ExError\`, \`ExErrorKind\`, and related error infrastructure from \`ettlex-core\` into a new standalone \`ettlex-errors\` crate\\n3. Retire \`EttleXError\` by migrating all usage to \`ExError\` across the workspace\\n4. Add four missing \`ExErrorKind\` variants: \`AlreadyTombstoned\`, \`SelfReferentialLink\`, \`HasActiveDependants\`, \`MissingLinkType\`\\n5. Update all \`Cargo.toml\` workspace dependencies to reflect the new crate structure\\n6. Verify \`ettlex-core-types\` content matches constraint definition\\n\\n## New crate: \`ettlex-errors\`\\n\\nContains:\\n- \`ExErrorKind\` enum with all variants \(including the four new ones\)\\n- \`ExError\` struct with all builder methods\\n- \`assert\_err\_kind!\` and \`assert\_err\_field!\` test macros\\n- \`From&lt;T&gt;\` conversions for \`rusqlite::Error\`, \`serde\_json::Error\`, \`std::io::Error\`\\n- NO dependency on \`ettlex-core\` or \`ettlex-logging\`\\n- Depends only on \`ettlex-core-types\`\\n\\nNew \`ExErrorKind\` variants:\\n- \`AlreadyTombstoned\` — operation attempted on a record whose \`tombstoned\_at\` is set; distinct from \`Deleted\` \(legacy boolean column\)\\n- \`SelfReferentialLink\` — \`reasoning\_link\_id\` set to the Ettle's own ID\\n- \`HasActiveDependants\` — tombstone blocked because active records reference this entity\\n- \`MissingLinkType\` — \`reasoning\_link\_id\` supplied without \`reasoning\_link\_type\`\\n\\nStable error codes for new variants:\\n- \`AlreadyTombstoned\` → \`ERR\_ALREADY\_TOMBSTONED\`\\n- \`SelfReferentialLink\` → \`ERR\_SELF\_REFERENTIAL\_LINK\`\\n- \`HasActiveDependants\` → \`ERR\_HAS\_ACTIVE\_DEPENDANTS\`\\n- \`MissingLinkType\` → \`ERR\_MISSING\_LINK\_TYPE\`\\n\\n## New crate: \`ettlex-logging\`\\n\\nContains:\\n- \`logging\_facility::init\(profile\)\` — single initialisation point\\n- \`Profile\` enum \(Development, Production\)\\n- \`log\_op\_start!\`, \`log\_op\_end!\`, \`log\_op\_error!\` macros\\n- \`TestCapture\`, \`CapturedEvent\`, \`init\_test\_capture\` — test capture mode\\n- Root span wrapper for boundary entrypoints\\n- Depends on \`ettlex-errors\` and \`ettlex-core-types\`\\n- Does NOT depend on \`ettlex-core\`\\n\\n## EttleXError retirement\\n\\n\`EttleXError\` is the legacy error enum in \`ettlex-core/src/errors.rs\`. It coexists with \`ExError\` via a \`From&lt;EttleXError&gt; for ExError\` bridge.\\n\\nThis slice retires \`EttleXError\` by:\\n- Migrating all internal \`ettlex-core\` code that produces \`EttleXError\` to produce \`ExError\` directly\\n- Migrating all \`ettlex-engine\`, \`ettlex-store\`, \`ettlex-mcp\` code that references \`EttleXError\` to use \`ExError\`\\n- Removing the \`EttleXError\` enum and its \`From\` bridge once all usages are migrated\\n- The \`Result&lt;T&gt;\` alias in \`ettlex-errors\` is \`std::result::Result&lt;T, ExError&gt;\`\\n\\n## Dependency graph after this slice\\n\\n\`\`\`\\nettlex-cli  ettlex-mcp  ettlex-tauri       \(entry points\)\\n        ↓         ↓           ↓\\n          ettlex-engine\\n               ↓\\n          ettlex-store\\n               ↓\\n          ettlex-core\\n               ↓\\n        ettlex-logging\\n               ↓\\n        ettlex-errors\\n               ↓\\n       ettlex-core-types        \(no workspace deps\)\\n\\nettlex-projection → ettlex-core only\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n## Workspace Cargo.toml changes\\n\\n- Add \`ettlex-errors\` and \`ettlex-logging\` to \`\[workspace\]\` members\\n- Add \`ettlex-errors\` and \`ettlex-logging\` to \`\[workspace.dependencies\]\`\\n- All crates that previously depended on \`ettlex-core\` for \`ExError\`/\`ExErrorKind\` must now depend on \`ettlex-errors\`\\n- All crates that previously depended on \`ettlex-core\` for logging must now depend on \`ettlex-logging\`\\n- \`ettlex-core\` depends on \`ettlex-logging\` and \`ettlex-errors\`\\n- \`ettlex-core/src/errors.rs\` retains only \`EttleXError\` retirement stubs \(empty or removed\) and re-exports from \`ettlex-errors\`\\n- \`ettlex-core/src/logging\_facility/\` is removed; \`ettlex-core\` imports from \`ettlex-logging\`\\n\\n## ettlex-core-types verification\\n\\nVerify the following are present and correct in \`ettlex-core-types\`:\\n- \`RequestId\`, \`TraceId\`, \`SpanId\` types \(correlation IDs\)\\n- \`RequestContext\` struct\\n- Canonical schema field key constants \(\`component\`, \`op\`, \`event\`, \`duration\_ms\`, \`request\_id\`, \`trace\_id\`, \`ettle\_id\`, \`err.kind\`, \`err.code\`\)\\n- \`Sensitive&lt;T&gt;\` marker and redaction helpers\\n- No subscriber initialisation, no IO, no logging dependency\\n\\nIf any of these are absent, add them as part of this slice.\\n\\n## Layer responsibilities \(unchanged by this slice\)\\n\\nNo business logic changes. No new user-visible behaviour. No schema changes. No MCP tool changes. This slice moves code to correct positions only.\\n\\n## Out of scope\\n\\n- Any feature work\\n- Schema migrations\\n- New MCP tools or commands\\n- Snapshot, decision, constraint, profile changes\\n- CLI wiring","why":"The EttleX codebase currently has two architectural violations that must be resolved before the vertical slice programme can proceed cleanly.\\n\\nFirst, \`logging\_facility\` is implemented as a module inside \`ettlex-core\` \(\`ettlex-core/src/logging\_facility/\`\). The logging constraint requires it to be a standalone crate that all other crates depend on. Having it inside \`ettlex-core\` inverts the dependency: crates that should sit below \`ettlex-core\` \(like \`ettlex-store\`\) cannot currently use the logging spine without taking a dependency on the full core domain model. This must be resolved before any slice introduces new logging calls.\\n\\nSecond, \`ExError\` and \`ExErrorKind\` are implemented inside \`ettlex-core/src/errors.rs\` alongside \`EttleXError\`, the legacy error enum. The error handling constraint requires \`error\_facility\` to be a standalone crate depending only on \`ettlex-core-types\`. Currently any crate that wants \`ExError\` must depend on all of \`ettlex-core\`. Additionally, \`EttleXError\` is a legacy enum that should be retired in favour of \`ExError\` across the codebase; having both creates confusion and drift.\\n\\nThird, the \`ExErrorKind\` taxonomy is missing four variants required by Slice 01: \`AlreadyTombstoned\`, \`SelfReferentialLink\`, \`HasActiveDependants\`, and \`MissingLinkType\`. These must be added here, not in Slice 01, so the error taxonomy is complete before feature work begins.\\n\\n\`ettlex-core-types\` already exists as a standalone crate in the correct position. No changes are needed to its structure, though its content should be verified against the constraint definition.\\n\\nThis infrastructure slice is a prerequisite for all subsequent vertical slices. It produces no new user-visible behaviour — it is a structural refactor that moves existing implementations to their correct positions in the dependency graph."} | 0 | 1773569280 | 1773569280 | null | ettle:019cf0f6-5797-73a3-895a-c42ef4f22e38 | Slice 00 — Infrastructure: logging\_facility + error\_facility crate extraction | null | 0 | 2026-03-15T10:06:42Z | 2026-03-15T10:06:42Z | {"data":{}} | null |  |  |  | null | null | null |

active dependants\\n  Given Ettle P, Ettle C with reasoning\_link\_id = P and C is not tombstoned\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: P }\\n  Then error kind HasActiveDependants is returned\\n  And ettle.get\(P\).tombstoned\_at is null\\n\\nScenario: EttleTombstone rejects non-existent Ettle\\n  When I apply EttleTombstone { ettle\_id: \\"ettle:missing\\" }\\n  Then error kind NotFound is returned\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Hard delete prohibition\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Hard delete is not exposed via MCP in this slice\\n  When I attempt to invoke any hard delete operation via ettlex.apply\\n  Then the command is not recognised\\n  And no row is deleted from the database\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: OCC\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Command with correct expected\_state\_version succeeds\\n  Given state\_version is V\\n  When I apply any write command with expected\_state\_version = V\\n  Then the command succeeds and new\_state\_version = V + 1\\n\\nScenario: Command with wrong expected\_state\_version fails\\n  Given state\_version is V\\n  When I apply any write command with expected\_state\_version = V - 1\\n  Then error kind HeadMismatch is returned\\n  And state\_version remains V\\n  And no provenance event is appended\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Provenance / observability\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: Each successful mutation appends exactly one provenance event\\n  When I apply any of EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone successfully\\n  Then exactly one provenance\_event row is appended\\n  And the event kind matches the command \(ettle\_created, ettle\_updated, ettle\_tombstoned\)\\n\\nScenario: Failed commands append no provenance events\\n  When I apply a command that returns any typed error\\n  Then no provenance\_event row is appended\\n  And the total provenance\_event count is unchanged\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Deterministic byte-level output\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleGet output is byte-identical across repeated calls\\n  Given Ettle E exists with all fields populated\\n  When I call ettle.get\(E\) twice without modifying state\\n  Then the JSON responses are byte-identical\\n  And field ordering in the JSON is stable\\n\\nScenario: EttleList output is byte-identical across repeated calls\\n  Given 5 Ettles exist\\n  When I call ettle.list\(\) twice without modifying state\\n  Then the JSON responses are byte-identical\\n  And item ordering is stable\\n\`\`\`\\n\\n### Feature: Resource limits\\n\\n\`\`\`gherkin\\nScenario: EttleCreate with large WHY/WHAT/HOW fields succeeds\\n  When I apply EttleCreate { title: \\"T\\", why: &lt;100KB string&gt;, what: &lt;100KB string&gt;, how: &lt;100KB string&gt; }\\n  Then the command succeeds within the enumerate each specific test function in the Pre-Authorised Failure Registry section of the completion report.","what":"## Scope\\n\\nThis slice implements full Ettle CRUD across Store, Engine/Action, and MCP layers:\\n- EttleCreate\\n- EttleGet\\n- EttleList \(paginated, deterministic\)\\n- EttleUpdate \(title, why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type\)\\n- EttleTombstone \(with dependant check\)\\n\\nHard delete is out of scope \(deferred pending Profile system\).\\nEP CRUD is out of scope.\\nRelation CRUD is out of scope \(Reasoning Link fields are stored on the Ettle record but the full Relation model is a future slice\).\\nAuthentication and authorisation are out of scope.\\nCLI wiring is out of scope.\\nSnapshot commit changes are out of scope.\\nDecision, Constraint, Group CRUD are out of scope.\\n\\n## Replacement targets\\n\\nThe following existing code is SUPERSEDED by this slice and MUST be replaced, not extended:\\n\\n### ettlex-mcp/src/tools/ettle.rs\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_get\` — superseded; new version returns full new field set including why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, tombstoned\_at\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_list\` — superseded; new version accepts include\_tombstoned, uses new field ordering, returns tombstoned\_at\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_list\_eps\` — retained as-is \(EP tooling, not in scope\)\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_list\_decisions\` — retained as-is \(not in scope\)\\n\\n### ettlex-engine/src/commands/mcp\_command.rs — EttleCreate and EttleUpdate dispatch\\n- \`McpCommand::EttleCreate\` variant — superseded; new variant accepts why/what/how/reasoning\_link\_id/reasoning\_link\_type; must not accept ettle\_id\\n- \`McpCommand::EttleUpdate\` variant — superseded; new variant accepts why/what/how/reasoning\_link\_id/reasoning\_link\_type; field-level patch semantics\\n- Dispatch arm for \`EttleCreate\` in \`dispatch\_mcp\_command\` — superseded; ALL invariant enforcement must move to a dedicated engine handler; dispatch arm becomes a thin delegation call only\\n- Dispatch arm for \`EttleUpdate\` in \`dispatch\_mcp\_command\` — superseded; same as above\\n- New variants to add: \`McpCommand::EttleTombstone\`, \`McpCommand::EttleGet\`, \`McpCommand::EttleList\`\\n- New result variants to add: \`McpCommandResult::EttleTombstone\`, \`McpCommandResult::EttleUpdate\` \(was missing\)\\n\\n### ettlex-store/src/repo/sqlite\_repo.rs — Ettle persistence\\n- \`persist\_ettle\` — superseded; must use new column set \(why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, tombstoned\_at\); must NOT write parent\_id, parent\_ep\_id, deleted, metadata\\n- \`persist\_ettle\_tx\` — superseded; same as above\\n- \`get\_ettle\` — superseded; must read new column set; must NOT read parent\_id, parent\_ep\_id, deleted, metadata\\n- \`list\_ettles\_paginated\` — superseded; must use new ordering \(created\_at ASC, id ASC\), support include\_tombstoned, use tombstoned\_at IS NULL filter, enforce limit min/max\\n\\n## Post-slice structural invariants\\n\\nThe following MUST hold after this slice is complete. These are verified by the architectural conformance scenarios.\\n\\nINV-1: \`dispatch\_mcp\_command\` MUST contain no Ettle business logic. For EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone, EttleGet, and EttleList, it MUST delegate entirely to engine handler functions. Existence checks, tombstone checks, invariant enforcement, and state\_version increment MUST NOT appear in the dispatch match arm.\\n\\nINV-2: Dedicated engine handler functions MUST exist for each operation:\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_create\(cmd, conn, cas\)\` in \`ettlex-engine\`\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_update\(cmd, conn, cas\)\` in \`ettlex-engine\`\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_tombstone\(cmd, conn\)\` in \`ettlex-engine\`\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_get\(ettle\_id, conn\)\` in \`ettlex-engine\`\\n- \`handle\_ettle\_list\(opts, conn\)\` in \`ettlex-engine\`\\n\\nINV-3: Store functions for Ettle operations MUST contain no domain rule validation. \`insert\_ettle\`, \`get\_ettle\`, \`list\_ettles\`, \`update\_ettle\`, \`tombstone\_ettle\` MUST perform only: SQL execution, FK existence checking via query, and rusqlite error conversion to ExError.\\n\\nINV-4: \`ettlex-mcp\` tool handlers for ettle.get and ettle.list MUST contain no invariant enforcement. They deserialise parameters and call engine query handlers only.\\n\\nINV-5: \`ettlex-mcp\` apply handler for EttleCreate, EttleUpdate, EttleTombstone MUST perform type/required-field validation only and delegate to engine command handlers.\\n\\nINV-6: state\_version increment \(INSERT INTO mcp\_command\_log\) MUST be performed by \`apply\_mcp\_command\` in \`ettlex-engine\`, not by any store function or MCP handler.\\n\\nINV-7: Provenance event append \(INSERT INTO provenance\_events\) MUST be performed by the engine action layer, not by any store function or MCP handler.\\n\\nINV-8: All new and migrated code in this slice MUST return \`Result&lt;T, ExError&gt;\` from \`ettlex-errors\`. No \`EttleXError\` references MUST appear in any file touched by this slice.\\n\\n## New Ettle Record Shape\\n\\nThe Ettle record at the store layer:\\n- id \(TEXT PRIMARY KEY, ettle: prefix, ULIDv7\)\\n- title \(TEXT NOT NULL\)\\n- why \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- what \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- how \(TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\)\\n- reasoning\_link\_id \(TEXT NULL, FK → ettles.id\)\\n- reasoning\_link\_type \(TEXT NULL\)\\n- created\_at \(TEXT NOT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n- updated\_at \(TEXT NOT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n- tombstoned\_at \(TEXT NULL, ISO-8601\)\\n\\nColumns removed: parent\_id, parent\_ep\_id, deleted, metadata\\n\\n## Migration\\n\\nA new numbered migration \(next after 011\) performs:\\n- ADD COLUMN why TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\\n- ADD COLUMN what TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\\n- ADD COLUMN how TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''\\n- ADD COLUMN reasoning\_link\_id TEXT NULL REFERENCES ettles\(id\)\\n- ADD COLUMN reasoning\_link\_type TEXT NULL\\n- ADD COLUMN tombstoned\_at TEXT NULL\\n- DROP COLUMN deleted\\n- DROP COLUMN parent\_id\\n- DROP COLUMN parent\_ep\_id\\n- DROP COLUMN metadata\\n- DROP INDEX idx\_ettles\_parent\_id \(if exists\)\\n- CREATE INDEX idx\_ettles\_reasoning\_link ON ettles\(reasoning\_link\_id\)\\n- CREATE INDEX idx\_ettles\_tombstoned ON ettles\(tombstoned\_at\)\\n\\nMigration MUST be additive for surviving data. All existing rows receive empty strings for why/what/how and NULL for reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, tombstoned\_at.\\n\\n## Command Vocabulary \(Action Layer\)\\n\\n### EttleCreate\\nInput: title \(required, non-empty after trimming\), why \(optional, default ''\), what \(optional, default ''\), how \(optional, default ''\), reasoning\_link\_id \(optional, nullable\), reasoning\_link\_type \(optional, nullable, required if reasoning\_link\_id is set\)\\nOutput: { ettle\_id }\\nInvariants \(all enforced in engine, not MCP or store\):\\n- title must be non-empty after trimming whitespace\\n- ettle\_id is auto-generated \(ULIDv7 prefixed ettle:\); caller MUST NOT supply ettle\_id\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is supplied, referenced Ettle must exist and must not be tombstoned\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is supplied, reasoning\_link\_type must also be supplied\\n- reasoning\_link\_type must be a non-empty string when supplied\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_created appended\\n\\n### EttleGet\\nInput: ettle\_id\\nOutput: { id, title, why, what, how, reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type, created\_at, updated\_at, tombstoned\_at }\\nInvariants:\\n- Returns NotFound if ettle\_id does not exist\\n- Returns the record including tombstoned records \(caller sees tombstoned\_at\)\\n- No state\_version increment \(read-only\)\\n- Repeated calls with identical state return byte-identical JSON output\\n\\n### EttleList\\nInput: limit \(optional, default 100, min 1, max 1000\), cursor \(optional, opaque base64\), include\_tombstoned \(optional bool, default false\)\\nOutput: { items: \[{ id, title, tombstoned\_at }\], cursor? }\\nInvariants:\\n- Ordering: \(created\_at ASC, id ASC\) — deterministic\\n- Excludes tombstoned records by default; include\_tombstoned=true includes them\\n- Cursor is opaque base64-encoded \(created\_at, id\) pair\\n- No state\_version increment \(read-only\)\\n- Repeated calls with identical parameters and identical state return byte-identical JSON output\\n- limit=1 is valid; limit=1000 is the maximum; limit=0 and limit≥1001 are rejected with InvalidInput\\n\\n### EttleUpdate\\nInput: ettle\_id \(required\), title \(optional\), why \(optional\), what \(optional\), how \(optional\), reasoning\_link\_id \(optional, null clears the link\), reasoning\_link\_type \(optional, null clears the type\)\\nOutput: {}\\nInvariants \(all enforced in engine\):\\n- At least one field must be supplied\\n- ettle\_id must exist and must not be tombstoned\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is set to a non-null value, referenced Ettle must exist and not be tombstoned\\n- An Ettle MUST NOT be set as its own reasoning\_link\_id \(SelfReferentialLink\)\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is cleared \(null\), reasoning\_link\_type is also cleared\\n- If reasoning\_link\_id is set to a non-null value, reasoning\_link\_type must be supplied and non-empty\\n- Unspecified optional fields are preserved unchanged\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_updated appended\\n\\n### EttleTombstone\\nInput: ettle\_id \(required\)\\nOutput: {}\\nInvariants \(all enforced in engine\):\\n- ettle\_id must exist and must not already be tombstoned \(AlreadyTombstoned\)\\n- Ettle must have no active \(non-tombstoned\) dependants: no other Ettle has reasoning\_link\_id = this ettle\_id where tombstoned\_at IS NULL\\n- Row is retained; tombstoned\_at is set to current UTC timestamp\\n- state\_version increments by 1\\n- Provenance event ettle\_tombstoned appended\\n\\n## Error Kinds Used\\n\\nAll from ExErrorKind in ettlex-errors \(all available after Slice 00\):\\n- InvalidInput — missing required fields, invalid limit values, caller-supplied ettle\_id, no fields in update\\n- InvalidTitle — title is empty or whitespace-only\\n- NotFound — ettle\_id does not exist\\n- AlreadyTombstoned — operation on a tombstoned Ettle; or referencing a tombstoned Ettle as reasoning\_link\_id\\n- SelfReferentialLink — reasoning\_link\_id set to own ettle\_id\\n- HasActiveDependants — EttleTombstone blocked by active child Ettles\\n- MissingLinkType — reasoning\_link\_id supplied without reasoning\_link\_type\\n- HeadMismatch — expected\_state\_version does not match current state\_version\\n\\n## Concurrency Model\\n\\nSQLite with rusqlite \(bundled\) serialises all write operations at the database level. The OCC mechanism via expected\_state\_version provides an additional application-level guard. No additional concurrency primitives are required in this slice.\\n\\n## Logging \(boundary ownership\)\\n\\nThe MCP entry point owns the lifecycle log events for each Ettle operation:\\n- log\_op\_start! at the top of each tool handler\\n- log\_op\_end! on success\\n- log\_op\_error! on any ExError return\\n\\nEngine handler functions MUST NOT emit lifecycle start/end events. They MAY emit DEBUG/TRACE events for internal steps. This conforms to the logging constraint boundary ownership rule.","why":"The existing Ettle CRUD implementation was written against the original schema and domain model. It conflates EP structure with Ettle identity, uses field names that no longer exist \(parent\_id, ettle\_id on EPs\), and lacks WHY/WHAT/HOW fields on the Ettle record itself. The new conceptual model \(v0.8\) places WHY, WHAT, and HOW directly on the Ettle record as the primary reasoning content, introduces a Reasoning Link \(reasoning\_link\_id, reasoning\_link\_type\) for parent traversal, and uses tombstoned\_at consistently across all governed records.\\n\\nThe vertical slice approach requires a full replacement of the Ettle CRUD path — Store, Engine/Action, and MCP — as a coherent unit. All layers must reflect the new model simultaneously. The existing implementations are replaced, not extended.\\n\\nThis slice has three concurrent objectives:\\n1. Implement the new Ettle record shape with WHY/WHAT/HOW and Reasoning Link fields\\n2. Migrate the architectural structure to match the layering constraint: business logic extracted from dispatch\_mcp\_command into dedicated engine handlers, MCP layer reduced to transport wiring only, store layer reduced to structural persistence only\\n3. Migrate the codebase from the legacy EttleXError where it appears in the Ettle CRUD path to ExError \(infrastructure from Slice 00\)\\n\\nPrerequisite: Slice 00 \(infrastructure\) MUST be complete before this slice runs. This slice assumes ettlex-errors and ettlex-logging crates exist, ExErrorKind includes AlreadyTombstoned/SelfReferentialLink/HasActiveDependants/MissingLinkType, and EttleXError is retired.\\n\\nHard delete is deferred: the Profile system required to govern it is not part of this slice. Tombstone is the only deletion path in this slice.\\n\\nEP CRUD is explicitly out of scope. EPs are a legacy construct being phased out; the new model stores reasoning content directly on the Ettle record."} | 0 | 1773569439 | 1773569439 | null | ettle:019cf0f7-ae6b-7ea3-8b72-ba0b4052b9c3 | Slice 01 — Ettle CRUD \(Store → Engine/Action → MCP\) v3 | null | 0 | 2026-03-15T10:08:09Z | 2026-03-15T10:08:09Z | {"data":{}} | null |  |  |  | null | null | null |
